  21:59:22.920  > --[[
	UltraScriptExporter – Clean Category Edition
	- Excludes Workspace and engine internals.
	- Plain ASCII output for maximum AI compatibility.
	- Clear section headers per container, then each script's metadata and source.
]]

local EXCLUDED_SERVICES = {
	["CoreGui"] = true,
	["RobloxReplicatedStorage"] = true,
	["ScriptContext"] = true,
	["ControllerService"] = true,
	["RealismService"] = true,
	["Workspace"] = true,   -- explicitly excluded as requested
}

local function GetScriptType(obj)
	local c = obj.ClassName
	if c == "Script" then return "Script"
	elseif c == "LocalScript" then return "LocalScript"
	elseif c == "ModuleScript" then return "Module"
	else return c
	end
end

local function SafeGetSource(obj)
	local ok, result = pcall(function() return obj.Source end)
	if ok then return result
	else return "-- ERROR reading source"
	end
end

-- Gather all top-level containers that contain scripts
local groups = {}
for _, child in ipairs(game:GetChildren()) do
	if child:IsA("Instance") and not EXCLUDED_SERVICES[child.ClassName] then
		local count = 0
		for _, desc in child:GetDescendants() do
			if desc:IsA("Script") or desc:IsA("LocalScript") or desc:IsA("ModuleScript") then
				count += 1
			end
		end
		if count > 0 then
			table.insert(groups, { container = child, name = child.Name, fullPath = child:GetFullName(), count = count })
		end
	end
end

table.sort(groups, function(a, b) return a.name < b.name end)

print("=================================================")
print("  FULL ROBLOX SCRIPT EXPORT (AI Ready)")
print("  Containers: " .. #groups)
print("=================================================")
print("")

local totalScripts = 0
local typeCount = { Script = 0, LocalScript = 0, Module = 0 }

for _, group in ipairs(groups) do
	-- Category header
	print("=================================================")
	print("  CATEGORY: " .. group.name)
	print("  Root Path: " .. group.fullPath)
	print("  Scripts: " .. group.count)
	print("=================================================")
	print("")

	for _, descendant in group.container:GetDescendants() do
		if descendant:IsA("Script") or descendant:IsA("LocalScript") or descendant:IsA("ModuleScript") then
			local scriptType = GetScriptType(descendant)
			local fullPath = descendant:GetFullName()
			local name = descendant.Name
			local enabled = true
			if scriptType == "Script" or scriptType == "LocalScript" then
				enabled = descendant.Enabled ~= false
			end
			local source = SafeGetSource(descendant)

			-- Simple script header
			print("--- " .. scriptType .. " : " .. name .. " ---")
			print("Path: " .. fullPath)
			if scriptType ~= "Module" then
				print("Enabled: " .. tostring(enabled))
			end
			print("---------- Source ----------")
			print(source)
			print("-----------------------------")
			print("")

			totalScripts += 1
			typeCount[scriptType] = (typeCount[scriptType] or 0) + 1
		end
	end
end

print("=================================================")
print("  EXPORT FINISHED")
print("  Total scripts: " .. totalScripts)
print("  Script: " .. (typeCount.Script or 0))
print("  LocalScript: " .. (typeCount.LocalScript or 0))
print("  Module: " .. (typeCount.Module or 0))
print("=================================================")
print(">> Copy above output and paste into AI.")  -  Studio

Abilities["Slash"] = {
	Cooldown = 2,
	ImageID = "rbxassetid://119416110512774",

	Action = function(player)
		if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then return end

		local inputLock = player:FindFirstChild("InputLocked")
		if not inputLock then return end
		inputLock.Value = true

		local character = player.Character
		local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
		local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end

		local assets = AssetHandler.GetAssets(player, "Killer", "user_004")
		
		local slashAnim = assets.Animations.Slash
		local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(slashAnim)

		local sound = assets.Sounds.Slash:Clone()
		sound.Parent = rootPart
		sound:Play()

		HitboxModule.Constant(
			player,
			rootPart,
			Vector3.new(5, 7, 7),
			Vector3.new(0, 0, -5),
			0.5,
			0.03,
			function(targetChar)
				print(targetChar.Name)
				targetChar.Humanoid:TakeDamage(20)
			end
		)
		animationTrack:Play()
		task.delay(1, function() sound:Destroy() end)
		if not StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
			inputLock.Value = false
		end
	end
}

Abilities["Quake"] = {
	Cooldown = 35,
	ImageID = "rbxassetid://12787168857",

	Action = function(player)
		if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then return end
		local inputLock = player:FindFirstChild("InputLocked")
		if not inputLock then return end
		inputLock.Value = true

		local character = player.Character
		if not character then return end

		local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end

		local assets = AssetHandler.GetAssets(player, "Killer", "user_004")
		local spawnAnim = assets.Animations.Spawn
		local animationTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(spawnAnim)

		local slashAnim = assets.Animations.Slash
		local animationTrack2 = humanoid:LoadAnimation(slashAnim)

		local bass = assets.Sounds.Bass:Clone()
		bass.Parent = rootPart

		local spawnp = assets.Sounds.Spawn:Clone()
		spawnp.Parent = rootPart

		local slash = assets.Sounds.Slash:Clone()
		slash.Parent = rootPart

		local slow = assets.Sounds.Slow:Clone()
		slow.Parent = rootPart
		
		animationTrack:Play()
		humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
		task.spawn(function()
			while wait() do
				if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
					animationTrack:Stop()
					return
				end
				task.wait(0.2)
			end
		end)
		
		for _, markerName in ipairs({ "Hit", "Hit2", "Hit3" }) do
			animationTrack:GetMarkerReachedSignal(markerName):Connect(function()
				local sound = assets.Sounds.GroundHit:Clone()
				sound.Parent = rootPart
				sound:Play()
				task.delay(0.5, function()
					sound:Destroy()
				end)
			end)
		end
		
		print("fires")
		
		
		
		animationTrack.Stopped:Wait()
		if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then return end
		
		slow:Play()
		Remotes.CameraShake:FireClient(player,"Explosion")		

		for _, otherPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if otherPlayer ~= player and otherPlayer.Character and otherPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				local dist = (otherPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - rootPart.Position).Magnitude
				if dist <= 100 then
					Remotes.CameraShake:FireClient(otherPlayer,"Explosion")		
					StatusEffects.ApplyEffect(otherPlayer, "Slowness", 3, 2)
				end
			end
		end
		for _, s in ipairs({ bass, slash, spawnp }) do
			s.Ended:Connect(function()
				if s and s.Parent then s:Destroy() end
			end)
		end
		
		if not StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
			humanoid.WalkSpeed = KillerChar.WalkSpeed.Value
			inputLock.Value = false
			return
		end	
	end
}

Abilities["Lunge"] = {
	Cooldown = 20,
	ImageID = "rbxassetid://13879658042",

	Action = function(player)
		if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then return end

		local inputLock = player:FindFirstChild("InputLocked")
		if not inputLock then return end
		inputLock.Value = true
		local character = player.Character
		local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
		local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end

		local assets = AssetHandler.GetAssets(player, "Killer", "user_004")
		local startupTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(assets.Animations.LungeStartup)
		local lungeTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(assets.Animations.Lunge)
		local missLunge = humanoid:LoadAnimation(assets.Animations.missLunge)
		local hitLunge = humanoid:LoadAnimation(assets.Animations.hitLunge)

		local lungesound = assets.Sounds.Lunge:Clone()
		lungesound.Parent = rootPart
		local whoosh = assets.Sounds.Whoosh:Clone()
		whoosh.Parent = rootPart

		StatusEffects.ApplyEffect(player, "Slowness", 0.8, 2)
		startupTrack:Play()
		print(startupTrack.Length)
		startupTrack.Stopped:Wait()

		if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
			inputLock.Value = false
			return
		end

		lungesound:Play()
		whoosh:Play()
		lungeTrack:Play()

		local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
		bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 0, 100000)
		bv.Velocity = Vector3.zero
		bv.Parent = rootPart

		local totalTime = 5
		local startSpeed = 10
		local maxSpeed = 60
		local startTime = tick()
		local runService = game:GetService("RunService")

		local rayParams = RaycastParams.new()
		rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude

		local ignoreList = {character}
		local hitboxFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Hitboxes")

		if hitboxFolder then
			table.insert(ignoreList, hitboxFolder)
		end
		
		if workspace:WaitForChild("Map"):FindFirstChild("KillerOnlyDoors") then
			table.insert(ignoreList, workspace:WaitForChild("Map"):FindFirstChild("KillerOnlyDoors"))
		end
		
		rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = ignoreList

		local connection
		local hitSomething = false

		local function stopLunge()
			if connection and connection.Connected then connection:Disconnect() end
			if bv then bv:Destroy() end
			lungeTrack:Stop()
			lungesound:Destroy()
			whoosh:Destroy()
			inputLock.Value = false
			if HitboxModule.StopConstant then
				HitboxModule.StopConstant()
			end

			if not StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
				if not hitSomething then
					print("Missed")
					StatusEffects.ApplyEffect(player, "EndLag", 2, 1)
					missLunge:Play()
				else
					print("Hit!")

					hitLunge:Play()
					StatusEffects.ApplyEffect(player, "Slowness", 1, 1)
				end
			end
		end

		task.spawn(function()
			while wait() do
				if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
					stopLunge()
					return
				end
				task.wait(0.1)
			end
		end)

		connection = runService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
			if not character or not rootPart or not humanoid then
				stopLunge()
				return
			end

			local elapsed = tick() - startTime
			local t = math.clamp(elapsed / totalTime, 0, 1)
			local speed = startSpeed + (maxSpeed - startSpeed) * (t ^ 1.5)

			local moveDir = humanoid.MoveDirection
			if moveDir.Magnitude < 0.1 then
				moveDir = rootPart.CFrame.LookVector
			end

			local rayOrigin = rootPart.Position
			local rayDirection = moveDir.Unit * 4
			local rayResult = workspace:Raycast(rayOrigin, rayDirection, rayParams)

			if rayResult and rayResult.Instance then
				hitSomething = true
				bv.Velocity *= 0.3
				local normal = rayResult.Normal
				rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(rootPart.Position + normal * 0.3, rootPart.Position + moveDir)
				task.delay(0.15, stopLunge)
				return
			end

			bv.Velocity = moveDir.Unit * speed

			if elapsed >= totalTime then
				stopLunge()
			end
		end)

		HitboxModule.Constant(
			player,
			rootPart,
			Vector3.new(6, 7, 3),
			Vector3.new(0, 0, -5),
			totalTime,
			0.05,
			function(targetChar)
				player.leaderstats.Tix.Value += 15
				Remotes.NotificationEvent:FireClient(player, "+15 Tix", "For Successfully hitting a Lunge")
				hitSomething = true
				targetChar.Humanoid:TakeDamage(25)
				print(player.Name .. " hit " .. targetChar.Name .. " with a lunge.")
				stopLunge()
			end
		)
	end
}



Abilities["Pierced"] = {
	Cooldown = 25,
	ImageID = "rbxassetid://13179744871",

	Action = function(player)
		local inputLock = player:FindFirstChild("InputLocked")
		if not inputLock then return end
		inputLock.Value = true

		local character = player.Character
		local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
		local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end
		humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
		local assets = AssetHandler.GetAssets(player, "Killer", "user_004")
		local stabAnim = assets.Animations.stab
		local stabTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(stabAnim)

		local soundStab = assets.Sounds.Ouch:Clone()
		local soundOverclock = assets.Sounds.Overclock:Clone()
		soundStab.Parent = rootPart
		soundOverclock.Parent = rootPart

		stabTrack:Play()
		soundOverclock:Play()
		task.spawn(function()
			while wait() do
				if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
					stabTrack:Stop()
					return
				end
				task.wait(0.2)
			end
		end)
		
		task.spawn(function()
			stabTrack:GetMarkerReachedSignal("Hit"):Wait()
			print("HitStab")
			soundStab:Play()
		end)
		
		stabTrack.Stopped:Wait()
		if StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then return end

		StatusEffects.ApplyEffect(player, "Haste", 5, 2)
		
		task.spawn(function()
			task.wait(5)
			StatusEffects.ApplyEffect(player, "Slowness", 3, 3)
		end)
		

		task.delay(6, function()
			soundStab:Destroy()
			soundOverclock:Destroy()
		end)

		if not StatusManager.HasStatus("Stunned", player) then
			humanoid.WalkSpeed = KillerChar.WalkSpeed.Value
			inputLock.Value = false
			return
		end
	end
}

return Abilities

local dances = {"dance1", "dance2", "dance3"}

-- Existance in this list signifies that it is an emote, the value indicates if it is a looping emote
local emoteNames = { wave = false, point = false, dance1 = true, dance2 = true, dance3 = true, laugh = false, cheer = false}

function isInjured()
	return Humanoid.Health < 50
end

function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
	if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then
		for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do
			connection:disconnect()
		end
	end
	animTable[name] = {}
	animTable[name].count = 0
	animTable[name].totalWeight = 0	
	animTable[name].connections = {}

	-- check for config values
	local config = script:FindFirstChild(name)
	if (config ~= nil) then
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		local idx = 1
		for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do
			if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then
				table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
				animTable[name][idx] = {}
				animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart
				local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight")
				if (weightObject == nil) then
					animTable[name][idx].weight = 1
				else
					animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value
				end
				animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
				animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight
				idx = idx + 1
			end
		end
	end

	-- fallback to defaults
	if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then
		for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do
			animTable[name][idx] = {}
			animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation")
			animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name
			animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id
			animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight
			animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
			animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight
		end
	end
end

-- Setup animation objects
function scriptChildModified(child)
	local fileList = animNames[child.Name]
	if (fileList ~= nil) then
		configureAnimationSet(child.Name, fileList)
	end	
end

script.ChildAdded:connect(scriptChildModified)
script.ChildRemoved:connect(scriptChildModified)

for name, fileList in pairs(animNames) do 
	configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
end	

-- ANIMATION

-- declarations
local toolAnim = "None"
local toolAnimTime = 0

local jumpAnimTime = 0
local jumpAnimDuration = 0.3

local toolTransitionTime = 0.1
local fallTransitionTime = 0.3
local jumpMaxLimbVelocity = 0.75

-- functions

function stopAllAnimations()
	local oldAnim = currentAnim

	-- return to idle if finishing an emote
	if (emoteNames[oldAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[oldAnim] == false) then
		oldAnim = "idle"
	end

	currentAnim = ""
	currentAnimInstance = nil
	if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		currentAnimTrack:Stop()
		currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		currentAnimTrack = nil
	end
	return oldAnim
end

function setAnimationSpeed(speed)
	if speed ~= currentAnimSpeed then
		currentAnimSpeed = speed
		currentAnimTrack:AdjustSpeed(currentAnimSpeed)
	end
end

function keyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then

		local repeatAnim = currentAnim
		-- return to idle if finishing an emote
		if (emoteNames[repeatAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[repeatAnim] == false) then
			repeatAnim = "idle"
		end

		local animSpeed = currentAnimSpeed
		playAnimation(repeatAnim, 0.0, Humanoid)
		setAnimationSpeed(animSpeed)
	end
end

-- Preload animations
function playAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid) 
	-- Check if injured and override animation if needed
	local actualAnimName = animName
	if isInjured() then
		if animName == "idle" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredidle"
		elseif animName == "walk" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredwalk"
		elseif animName == "run" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredrun"
		end
	end

	if animTable[actualAnimName] == nil then
		-- Fallback to regular animation if injured version doesn't exist
		actualAnimName = animName
	end

	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[actualAnimName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[actualAnimName][idx].anim

	-- switch animation		
	if (anim ~= currentAnimInstance) then

		if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			currentAnimTrack:Stop(transitionTime)
			currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		end

		currentAnimSpeed = 1.0

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		currentAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		currentAnimTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Core

		-- play the animation
		currentAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		currentAnim = actualAnimName
		currentAnimInstance = anim

		-- set up keyframe name triggers
		if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
			currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
		end
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler = currentAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(keyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

local toolAnimName = ""
local toolAnimTrack = nil
local toolAnimInstance = nil
local currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = nil

function toolKeyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then
		playToolAnimation(toolAnimName, 0.0, Humanoid)
	end
end

function playToolAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid, priority)	 
	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[animName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[animName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[animName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[animName][idx].anim

	if (toolAnimInstance ~= anim) then
		if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			toolAnimTrack:Stop()
			toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
			transitionTime = 0
		end

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		toolAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		if priority then
			toolAnimTrack.Priority = priority
		end

		-- play the animation
		toolAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		toolAnimName = animName
		toolAnimInstance = anim

		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = toolAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(toolKeyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

function stopToolAnimations()
	local oldAnim = toolAnimName

	if (currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	toolAnimName = ""
	toolAnimInstance = nil
	if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		toolAnimTrack:Stop()
		toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
		toolAnimTrack = nil
	end

	return oldAnim
end

function onRunning(speed)
	RunningSpeed = speed
	if speed > 0.01 then
		if speed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run", 0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
		if currentAnimInstance and (currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=180426354" or 
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=252557606" or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredwalk[1].id or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredrun[1].id) then
			if speed > 20 then
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 29.0)
			else
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 14.5)
			end
		end
		pose = "Running"
	else
		if emoteNames[currentAnim] == nil then
			playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
			pose = "Standing"
		end
	end
end

function onDied()
	pose = "Dead"
end

function onJumping()
	playAnimation("jump", 0.1, Humanoid)
	jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimDuration
	pose = "Jumping"
end

function onClimbing(speed)
	playAnimation("climb", 0.1, Humanoid)
	setAnimationSpeed(speed / 12.0)
	pose = "Climbing"
end

function onGettingUp()
	pose = "GettingUp"
end

function onFreeFall()
	if (jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	end
	pose = "FreeFall"
end

function onFallingDown()
	pose = "FallingDown"
end

function onSeated()
	pose = "Seated"
end

function onPlatformStanding()
	pose = "PlatformStanding"
end

function onSwimming(speed)
	if speed > 0 then
		pose = "Running"
	else
		pose = "Standing"
	end
end

function getTool()	
	for _, kid in ipairs(Figure:GetChildren()) do
		if kid.className == "Tool" then return kid end
	end
	return nil
end

function getToolAnim(tool)
	for _, c in ipairs(tool:GetChildren()) do
		if c.Name == "toolanim" and c.className == "StringValue" then
			return c
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function animateTool()
	if (toolAnim == "None") then
		playToolAnimation("toolnone", toolTransitionTime, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Idle)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Slash") then
		playToolAnimation("toolslash", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Lunge") then
		playToolAnimation("toollunge", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end
end

function moveSit()
	RightShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	LeftShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
	RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
end

local lastTick = 0

function move(time)
	local amplitude = 1
	local frequency = 1
	local deltaTime = time - lastTick
	lastTick = time

	local climbFudge = 0
	local setAngles = false

	if (jumpAnimTime > 0) then
		jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimTime - deltaTime
	end

	if (pose == "FreeFall" and jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	elseif (pose == "Seated") then
		playAnimation("sit", 0.5, Humanoid)
		return
	elseif (pose == "Running") then
		if RunningSpeed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run",0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
	elseif (pose == "Dead" or pose == "GettingUp" or pose == "FallingDown" or pose == "Seated" or pose == "PlatformStanding") then
		stopAllAnimations()
		amplitude = 0.1
		frequency = 1
		setAngles = true
	end

	if (setAngles) then
		local desiredAngle = amplitude * math.sin(time * frequency)

		RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle + climbFudge)
		LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle - climbFudge)
		RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
		LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
	end

	-- Tool Animation handling
	local tool = getTool()
	if tool and tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
		local animStringValueObject = getToolAnim(tool)

		if animStringValueObject then
			toolAnim = animStringValueObject.Value
			animStringValueObject.Parent = nil
			toolAnimTime = time + .3
		end

		if time > toolAnimTime then
			toolAnimTime = 0
			toolAnim = "None"
		end

		animateTool()		
	else
		stopToolAnimations()
		toolAnim = "None"
		toolAnimInstance = nil
		toolAnimTime = 0
	end
end

-- connect events
Humanoid.Died:connect(onDied)
Humanoid.Running:connect(onRunning)
Humanoid.Jumping:connect(onJumping)
Humanoid.Climbing:connect(onClimbing)
Humanoid.GettingUp:connect(onGettingUp)
Humanoid.FreeFalling:connect(onFreeFall)
Humanoid.FallingDown:connect(onFallingDown)
Humanoid.Seated:connect(onSeated)
Humanoid.PlatformStanding:connect(onPlatformStanding)
Humanoid.Swimming:connect(onSwimming)

-- setup emote chat hook
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Chatted:connect(function(msg)
	local emote = ""
	if msg == "/e dance" then
		emote = dances[math.random(1, #dances)]
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 3) == "/e ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 4)
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 7) == "/emote ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 8)
	end

	if (pose == "Standing" and emoteNames[emote] ~= nil) then
		playAnimation(emote, 0.1, Humanoid)
	end
end)

-- initialize to idle
playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
pose = "Standing"

while Figure.Parent ~= nil do
	local _, time = wait(0.1)
	move(time)

local dances = {"dance1", "dance2", "dance3"}

-- Existance in this list signifies that it is an emote, the value indicates if it is a looping emote
local emoteNames = { wave = false, point = false, dance1 = true, dance2 = true, dance3 = true, laugh = false, cheer = false}

function isInjured()
	return Humanoid.Health < 50
end

function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
	if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then
		for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do
			connection:disconnect()
		end
	end
	animTable[name] = {}
	animTable[name].count = 0
	animTable[name].totalWeight = 0	
	animTable[name].connections = {}

	-- check for config values
	local config = script:FindFirstChild(name)
	if (config ~= nil) then
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		local idx = 1
		for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do
			if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then
				table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
				animTable[name][idx] = {}
				animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart
				local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight")
				if (weightObject == nil) then
					animTable[name][idx].weight = 1
				else
					animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value
				end
				animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
				animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight
				idx = idx + 1
			end
		end
	end

	-- fallback to defaults
	if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then
		for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do
			animTable[name][idx] = {}
			animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation")
			animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name
			animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id
			animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight
			animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
			animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight
		end
	end
end

-- Setup animation objects
function scriptChildModified(child)
	local fileList = animNames[child.Name]
	if (fileList ~= nil) then
		configureAnimationSet(child.Name, fileList)
	end	
end

script.ChildAdded:connect(scriptChildModified)
script.ChildRemoved:connect(scriptChildModified)

for name, fileList in pairs(animNames) do 
	configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
end	

-- ANIMATION

-- declarations
local toolAnim = "None"
local toolAnimTime = 0

local jumpAnimTime = 0
local jumpAnimDuration = 0.3

local toolTransitionTime = 0.1
local fallTransitionTime = 0.3
local jumpMaxLimbVelocity = 0.75

-- functions

function stopAllAnimations()
	local oldAnim = currentAnim

	-- return to idle if finishing an emote
	if (emoteNames[oldAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[oldAnim] == false) then
		oldAnim = "idle"
	end

	currentAnim = ""
	currentAnimInstance = nil
	if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		currentAnimTrack:Stop()
		currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		currentAnimTrack = nil
	end
	return oldAnim
end

function setAnimationSpeed(speed)
	if speed ~= currentAnimSpeed then
		currentAnimSpeed = speed
		currentAnimTrack:AdjustSpeed(currentAnimSpeed)
	end
end

function keyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then

		local repeatAnim = currentAnim
		-- return to idle if finishing an emote
		if (emoteNames[repeatAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[repeatAnim] == false) then
			repeatAnim = "idle"
		end

		local animSpeed = currentAnimSpeed
		playAnimation(repeatAnim, 0.0, Humanoid)
		setAnimationSpeed(animSpeed)
	end
end

-- Preload animations
function playAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid) 
	-- Check if injured and override animation if needed
	local actualAnimName = animName
	if isInjured() then
		if animName == "idle" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredidle"
		elseif animName == "walk" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredwalk"
		elseif animName == "run" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredrun"
		end
	end

	if animTable[actualAnimName] == nil then
		-- Fallback to regular animation if injured version doesn't exist
		actualAnimName = animName
	end

	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[actualAnimName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[actualAnimName][idx].anim

	-- switch animation		
	if (anim ~= currentAnimInstance) then

		if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			currentAnimTrack:Stop(transitionTime)
			currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		end

		currentAnimSpeed = 1.0

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		currentAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		currentAnimTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Core

		-- play the animation
		currentAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		currentAnim = actualAnimName
		currentAnimInstance = anim

		-- set up keyframe name triggers
		if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
			currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
		end
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler = currentAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(keyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
	elseif (pose == "Dead" or pose == "GettingUp" or pose == "FallingDown" or pose == "Seated" or pose == "PlatformStanding") then
		stopAllAnimations()
		amplitude = 0.1
		frequency = 1
		setAngles = true
	end

	if (setAngles) then
		local desiredAngle = amplitude * math.sin(time * frequency)

		RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle + climbFudge)
		LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle - climbFudge)
		RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
		LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
	end

	-- Tool Animation handling
	local tool = getTool()
	if tool and tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
		local animStringValueObject = getToolAnim(tool)

		if animStringValueObject then
			toolAnim = animStringValueObject.Value
			animStringValueObject.Parent = nil
			toolAnimTime = time + .3
		end

		if time > toolAnimTime then
			toolAnimTime = 0
			toolAnim = "None"
		end

		animateTool()		
	else
		stopToolAnimations()
		toolAnim = "None"
		toolAnimInstance = nil
		toolAnimTime = 0
	end
end

-- connect events
Humanoid.Died:connect(onDied)
Humanoid.Running:connect(onRunning)
Humanoid.Jumping:connect(onJumping)
Humanoid.Climbing:connect(onClimbing)
Humanoid.GettingUp:connect(onGettingUp)
Humanoid.FreeFalling:connect(onFreeFall)
Humanoid.FallingDown:connect(onFallingDown)
Humanoid.Seated:connect(onSeated)
Humanoid.PlatformStanding:connect(onPlatformStanding)
Humanoid.Swimming:connect(onSwimming)

-- setup emote chat hook
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Chatted:connect(function(msg)
	local emote = ""
	if msg == "/e dance" then
		emote = dances[math.random(1, #dances)]
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 3) == "/e ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 4)
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 7) == "/emote ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 8)
	end

	if (pose == "Standing" and emoteNames[emote] ~= nil) then
		playAnimation(emote, 0.1, Humanoid)
	end
end)

-- initialize to idle
playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
pose = "Standing"

	local _, time = wait(0.1)
	move(time)

	Cooldown = 20,
	ImageID = "rbxassetid://15760755440",
	Action = function(player)
		local inputLock = player:FindFirstChild("InputLocked")
		if not inputLock then return end

		Chezburger.Parent = workspace
		Chezburger.CanCollide = true

		local hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		Chezburger.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + hrp.CFrame.LookVector * 1 + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)

		local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
		bv.Velocity = hrp.CFrame.LookVector * 50 + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
		bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(4000, 4000, 4000)
		bv.Parent = Chezburger

		sound:Play()
		inputLock.Value = false

		task.delay(0.1, function()
			if bv and bv.Parent then
				bv:Destroy()
			end
		end)
		
		local touchedConnection
		touchedConnection = Chezburger.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
			local hitHumanoid = hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
			if hitHumanoid and hit.Parent.Name ~= player.Name then
				local hitPlayer = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(hit.Parent)
				if hitPlayer and not hitPlayer:FindFirstChild("Killer") then
					hit = true
					local nomnom = assets.Sounds.NomNom:Clone()
					nomnom.Parent = hitPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
					nomnom:Play()
					hitHumanoid.Health = math.min(hitHumanoid.MaxHealth, hitHumanoid.Health + 25)
					touchedConnection:Disconnect()
					Chezburger:Destroy()
				end
			end
		end)
		
		if hit == true then
			player.leaderstats.Tix.Value += 20

			Remotes.NotificationEvent:FireClient(player, "+20 Tix", "For Healing a Teammate")
		end
		task.delay(1, function()
			hit = false
		end)
		task.delay(10, function()
			if Chezburger and Chezburger.Parent then
				if touchedConnection then touchedConnection:Disconnect() end
				Chezburger:Destroy()
				sound:Destroy()
			end
		end)
	end
}

return Abilities

local dances = {"dance1", "dance2", "dance3"}

-- Existance in this list signifies that it is an emote, the value indicates if it is a looping emote
local emoteNames = { wave = false, point = false, dance1 = true, dance2 = true, dance3 = true, laugh = false, cheer = false}

function isInjured()
	return Humanoid.Health < 50
end

function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
	if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then
		for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do
			connection:disconnect()
		end
	end
	animTable[name] = {}
	animTable[name].count = 0
	animTable[name].totalWeight = 0	
	animTable[name].connections = {}

	-- check for config values
	local config = script:FindFirstChild(name)
	if (config ~= nil) then
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		local idx = 1
		for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do
			if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then
				table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
				animTable[name][idx] = {}
				animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart
				local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight")
				if (weightObject == nil) then
					animTable[name][idx].weight = 1
				else
					animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value
				end
				animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
				animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight
				idx = idx + 1
			end
		end
	end

	-- fallback to defaults
	if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then
		for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do
			animTable[name][idx] = {}
			animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation")
			animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name
			animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id
			animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight
			animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
			animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight
		end
	end
end

-- Setup animation objects
function scriptChildModified(child)
	local fileList = animNames[child.Name]
	if (fileList ~= nil) then
		configureAnimationSet(child.Name, fileList)
	end	
end

script.ChildAdded:connect(scriptChildModified)
script.ChildRemoved:connect(scriptChildModified)

for name, fileList in pairs(animNames) do 
	configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
end	

-- ANIMATION

-- declarations
local toolAnim = "None"
local toolAnimTime = 0

local jumpAnimTime = 0
local jumpAnimDuration = 0.3

local toolTransitionTime = 0.1
local fallTransitionTime = 0.3
local jumpMaxLimbVelocity = 0.75

-- functions

function stopAllAnimations()
	local oldAnim = currentAnim

	-- return to idle if finishing an emote
	if (emoteNames[oldAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[oldAnim] == false) then
		oldAnim = "idle"
	end

	currentAnim = ""
	currentAnimInstance = nil
	if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		currentAnimTrack:Stop()
		currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		currentAnimTrack = nil
	end
	return oldAnim
end

function setAnimationSpeed(speed)
	if speed ~= currentAnimSpeed then
		currentAnimSpeed = speed
		currentAnimTrack:AdjustSpeed(currentAnimSpeed)
	end
end

function keyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then

		local repeatAnim = currentAnim
		-- return to idle if finishing an emote
		if (emoteNames[repeatAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[repeatAnim] == false) then
			repeatAnim = "idle"
		end

		local animSpeed = currentAnimSpeed
		playAnimation(repeatAnim, 0.0, Humanoid)
		setAnimationSpeed(animSpeed)
	end
end

-- Preload animations
function playAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid) 
	-- Check if injured and override animation if needed
	local actualAnimName = animName
	if isInjured() then
		if animName == "idle" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredidle"
		elseif animName == "walk" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredwalk"
		elseif animName == "run" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredrun"
		end
	end

	if animTable[actualAnimName] == nil then
		-- Fallback to regular animation if injured version doesn't exist
		actualAnimName = animName
	end

	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[actualAnimName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[actualAnimName][idx].anim

	-- switch animation		
	if (anim ~= currentAnimInstance) then

		if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			currentAnimTrack:Stop(transitionTime)
			currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		end

		currentAnimSpeed = 1.0

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		currentAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		currentAnimTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Core

		-- play the animation
		currentAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		currentAnim = actualAnimName
		currentAnimInstance = anim

		-- set up keyframe name triggers
		if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
			currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
		end
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler = currentAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(keyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

local toolAnimName = ""
local toolAnimTrack = nil
local toolAnimInstance = nil
local currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = nil

function toolKeyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then
		playToolAnimation(toolAnimName, 0.0, Humanoid)
	end
end

function playToolAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid, priority)	 
	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[animName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[animName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[animName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[animName][idx].anim

	if (toolAnimInstance ~= anim) then
		if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			toolAnimTrack:Stop()
			toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
			transitionTime = 0
		end

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		toolAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		if priority then
			toolAnimTrack.Priority = priority
		end

		-- play the animation
		toolAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		toolAnimName = animName
		toolAnimInstance = anim

		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = toolAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(toolKeyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

function stopToolAnimations()
	local oldAnim = toolAnimName

	if (currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	toolAnimName = ""
	toolAnimInstance = nil
	if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		toolAnimTrack:Stop()
		toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
		toolAnimTrack = nil
	end

	return oldAnim
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function onRunning(speed)
	RunningSpeed = speed
	if speed > 0.01 then
		if speed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run", 0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
		if currentAnimInstance and (currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=180426354" or 
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=252557606" or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredwalk[1].id or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredrun[1].id) then
			if speed > 20 then
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 29.0)
			else
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 14.5)
			end
		end
		pose = "Running"
	else
		if emoteNames[currentAnim] == nil then
			playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
			pose = "Standing"
		end
	end
end

function onDied()
	pose = "Dead"
end

function onJumping()
	playAnimation("jump", 0.1, Humanoid)
	jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimDuration
	pose = "Jumping"
end

function onClimbing(speed)
	playAnimation("climb", 0.1, Humanoid)
	setAnimationSpeed(speed / 12.0)
	pose = "Climbing"
end

function onGettingUp()
	pose = "GettingUp"
end

function onFreeFall()
	if (jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	end
	pose = "FreeFall"
end

function onFallingDown()
	pose = "FallingDown"
end

function onSeated()
	pose = "Seated"
end

function onPlatformStanding()
	pose = "PlatformStanding"
end

function onSwimming(speed)
	if speed > 0 then
		pose = "Running"
	else
		pose = "Standing"
	end
end

function getTool()	
	for _, kid in ipairs(Figure:GetChildren()) do
		if kid.className == "Tool" then return kid end
	end
	return nil
end

function getToolAnim(tool)
	for _, c in ipairs(tool:GetChildren()) do
		if c.Name == "toolanim" and c.className == "StringValue" then
			return c
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function animateTool()
	if (toolAnim == "None") then
		playToolAnimation("toolnone", toolTransitionTime, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Idle)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Slash") then
		playToolAnimation("toolslash", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Lunge") then
		playToolAnimation("toollunge", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end
end

function moveSit()
	RightShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	LeftShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
	RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
end

local lastTick = 0

function move(time)
	local amplitude = 1
	local frequency = 1
	local deltaTime = time - lastTick
	lastTick = time

	local climbFudge = 0
	local setAngles = false

	if (jumpAnimTime > 0) then
		jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimTime - deltaTime
	end

	if (pose == "FreeFall" and jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	elseif (pose == "Seated") then
		playAnimation("sit", 0.5, Humanoid)
		return
	elseif (pose == "Running") then
		if RunningSpeed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run",0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
	elseif (pose == "Dead" or pose == "GettingUp" or pose == "FallingDown" or pose == "Seated" or pose == "PlatformStanding") then
		stopAllAnimations()
		amplitude = 0.1
		frequency = 1
		setAngles = true
	end

	if (setAngles) then
		local desiredAngle = amplitude * math.sin(time * frequency)

		RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle + climbFudge)
		LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle - climbFudge)
		RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
		LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
	end

	-- Tool Animation handling
	local tool = getTool()
	if tool and tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
		local animStringValueObject = getToolAnim(tool)

		if animStringValueObject then
			toolAnim = animStringValueObject.Value
			animStringValueObject.Parent = nil
			toolAnimTime = time + .3
		end

		if time > toolAnimTime then
			toolAnimTime = 0
			toolAnim = "None"
		end

		animateTool()		
	else
		stopToolAnimations()
		toolAnim = "None"
		toolAnimInstance = nil
		toolAnimTime = 0
	end
end

-- connect events
Humanoid.Died:connect(onDied)
Humanoid.Running:connect(onRunning)
Humanoid.Jumping:connect(onJumping)
Humanoid.Climbing:connect(onClimbing)
Humanoid.GettingUp:connect(onGettingUp)
Humanoid.FreeFalling:connect(onFreeFall)
Humanoid.FallingDown:connect(onFallingDown)
Humanoid.Seated:connect(onSeated)
Humanoid.PlatformStanding:connect(onPlatformStanding)
Humanoid.Swimming:connect(onSwimming)

-- setup emote chat hook
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Chatted:connect(function(msg)
	local emote = ""
	if msg == "/e dance" then
		emote = dances[math.random(1, #dances)]
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 3) == "/e ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 4)
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 7) == "/emote ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 8)
	end

	if (pose == "Standing" and emoteNames[emote] ~= nil) then
		playAnimation(emote, 0.1, Humanoid)
	end
end)

local dances = {"dance1", "dance2", "dance3"}

-- Existance in this list signifies that it is an emote, the value indicates if it is a looping emote
local emoteNames = { wave = false, point = false, dance1 = true, dance2 = true, dance3 = true, laugh = false, cheer = false}

function isInjured()
	return Humanoid.Health < 50
end

function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
	if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then
		for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do
			connection:disconnect()
		end
	end
	animTable[name] = {}
	animTable[name].count = 0
	animTable[name].totalWeight = 0	
	animTable[name].connections = {}

	-- check for config values
	local config = script:FindFirstChild(name)
	if (config ~= nil) then
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		local idx = 1
		for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do
			if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then
				table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
				animTable[name][idx] = {}
				animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart
				local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight")
				if (weightObject == nil) then
					animTable[name][idx].weight = 1
				else
					animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value
				end
				animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
				animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight
				idx = idx + 1
			end
		end
	end

	-- fallback to defaults
	if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then
		for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do
			animTable[name][idx] = {}
			animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation")
			animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name
			animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id
			animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight
			animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
			animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight
		end
	end
end

-- Setup animation objects
function scriptChildModified(child)
	local fileList = animNames[child.Name]
	if (fileList ~= nil) then
		configureAnimationSet(child.Name, fileList)
	end	
end

script.ChildAdded:connect(scriptChildModified)
script.ChildRemoved:connect(scriptChildModified)

for name, fileList in pairs(animNames) do 
	configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
end	

-- ANIMATION

-- declarations
local toolAnim = "None"
local toolAnimTime = 0

local jumpAnimTime = 0
local jumpAnimDuration = 0.3

local toolTransitionTime = 0.1
local fallTransitionTime = 0.3
local jumpMaxLimbVelocity = 0.75

-- functions

function stopAllAnimations()
	local oldAnim = currentAnim

	-- return to idle if finishing an emote
	if (emoteNames[oldAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[oldAnim] == false) then
		oldAnim = "idle"
	end

	currentAnim = ""
	currentAnimInstance = nil
	if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		currentAnimTrack:Stop()
		currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		currentAnimTrack = nil
	end
	return oldAnim
end

function setAnimationSpeed(speed)
	if speed ~= currentAnimSpeed then
		currentAnimSpeed = speed
		currentAnimTrack:AdjustSpeed(currentAnimSpeed)
	end
end

function keyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then

		local repeatAnim = currentAnim
		-- return to idle if finishing an emote
		if (emoteNames[repeatAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[repeatAnim] == false) then
			repeatAnim = "idle"
		end

		local animSpeed = currentAnimSpeed
		playAnimation(repeatAnim, 0.0, Humanoid)
		setAnimationSpeed(animSpeed)
	end
end

-- Preload animations
function playAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid) 
	-- Check if injured and override animation if needed
	local actualAnimName = animName
	if isInjured() then
		if animName == "idle" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredidle"
		elseif animName == "walk" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredwalk"
		elseif animName == "run" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredrun"
		end
	end

	if animTable[actualAnimName] == nil then
		-- Fallback to regular animation if injured version doesn't exist
		actualAnimName = animName
	end

	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[actualAnimName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[actualAnimName][idx].anim

	-- switch animation		
	if (anim ~= currentAnimInstance) then

		if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			currentAnimTrack:Stop(transitionTime)
			currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		end

		currentAnimSpeed = 1.0

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		currentAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		currentAnimTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Core

		-- play the animation
		currentAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		currentAnim = actualAnimName
		currentAnimInstance = anim

		-- set up keyframe name triggers
		if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
			currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
		end
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler = currentAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(keyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

local toolAnimName = ""
local toolAnimTrack = nil
local toolAnimInstance = nil
local currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = nil

function toolKeyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then
		playToolAnimation(toolAnimName, 0.0, Humanoid)
	end
end

function playToolAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid, priority)	 
	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[animName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[animName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[animName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[animName][idx].anim

	if (toolAnimInstance ~= anim) then
		if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			toolAnimTrack:Stop()
			toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
			transitionTime = 0
		end

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		toolAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		if priority then
			toolAnimTrack.Priority = priority
		end

		-- play the animation
		toolAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		toolAnimName = animName
		toolAnimInstance = anim

		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = toolAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(toolKeyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

function stopToolAnimations()
	local oldAnim = toolAnimName

	if (currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	toolAnimName = ""
	toolAnimInstance = nil
	if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		toolAnimTrack:Stop()
		toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
		toolAnimTrack = nil
	end

	return oldAnim
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function onRunning(speed)
	RunningSpeed = speed
	if speed > 0.01 then
		if speed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run", 0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
		if currentAnimInstance and (currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=180426354" or 
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=252557606" or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredwalk[1].id or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredrun[1].id) then
			if speed > 20 then
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 29.0)
			else
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 14.5)
			end
		end
		pose = "Running"
	else
		if emoteNames[currentAnim] == nil then
			playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
			pose = "Standing"
		end
	end
end

function onDied()
	pose = "Dead"
end

function onJumping()
	playAnimation("jump", 0.1, Humanoid)
	jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimDuration
	pose = "Jumping"
end

function onClimbing(speed)
	playAnimation("climb", 0.1, Humanoid)
	setAnimationSpeed(speed / 12.0)
	pose = "Climbing"
end

function onGettingUp()
	pose = "GettingUp"
end

function onFreeFall()
	if (jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	end
	pose = "FreeFall"
end

function onFallingDown()
	pose = "FallingDown"
end

function onSeated()
	pose = "Seated"
end

function onPlatformStanding()
	pose = "PlatformStanding"
end

function onSwimming(speed)
	if speed > 0 then
		pose = "Running"
	else
		pose = "Standing"
	end
end

function getTool()	
	for _, kid in ipairs(Figure:GetChildren()) do
		if kid.className == "Tool" then return kid end
	end
	return nil
end

function getToolAnim(tool)
	for _, c in ipairs(tool:GetChildren()) do
		if c.Name == "toolanim" and c.className == "StringValue" then
			return c
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function animateTool()
	if (toolAnim == "None") then
		playToolAnimation("toolnone", toolTransitionTime, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Idle)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Slash") then
		playToolAnimation("toolslash", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Lunge") then
		playToolAnimation("toollunge", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end
end

function moveSit()
	RightShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	LeftShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
	RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
end

local lastTick = 0

function move(time)
	local amplitude = 1
	local frequency = 1
	local deltaTime = time - lastTick
	lastTick = time

	local climbFudge = 0
	local setAngles = false

	if (jumpAnimTime > 0) then
		jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimTime - deltaTime
	end

	if (pose == "FreeFall" and jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	elseif (pose == "Seated") then
		playAnimation("sit", 0.5, Humanoid)
		return
	elseif (pose == "Running") then
		if RunningSpeed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run",0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
	elseif (pose == "Dead" or pose == "GettingUp" or pose == "FallingDown" or pose == "Seated" or pose == "PlatformStanding") then
		stopAllAnimations()
		amplitude = 0.1
		frequency = 1
		setAngles = true
	end

	if (setAngles) then
		local desiredAngle = amplitude * math.sin(time * frequency)

		RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle + climbFudge)
		LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle - climbFudge)
		RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
		LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
	end

	-- Tool Animation handling
	local tool = getTool()
	if tool and tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
		local animStringValueObject = getToolAnim(tool)

		if animStringValueObject then
			toolAnim = animStringValueObject.Value
			animStringValueObject.Parent = nil
			toolAnimTime = time + .3
		end

		if time > toolAnimTime then
			toolAnimTime = 0
			toolAnim = "None"
		end

		animateTool()		
	else
		stopToolAnimations()
		toolAnim = "None"
		toolAnimInstance = nil
		toolAnimTime = 0
	end
end

-- connect events
Humanoid.Died:connect(onDied)
Humanoid.Running:connect(onRunning)
Humanoid.Jumping:connect(onJumping)
Humanoid.Climbing:connect(onClimbing)
Humanoid.GettingUp:connect(onGettingUp)
Humanoid.FreeFalling:connect(onFreeFall)
Humanoid.FallingDown:connect(onFallingDown)
Humanoid.Seated:connect(onSeated)
Humanoid.PlatformStanding:connect(onPlatformStanding)
Humanoid.Swimming:connect(onSwimming)

-- setup emote chat hook
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Chatted:connect(function(msg)
	local emote = ""
	if msg == "/e dance" then
		emote = dances[math.random(1, #dances)]
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 3) == "/e ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 4)
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 7) == "/emote ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 8)
	end

	if (pose == "Standing" and emoteNames[emote] ~= nil) then
		playAnimation(emote, 0.1, Humanoid)
	end
end)

-- initialize to idle
playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
pose = "Standing"

while Figure.Parent ~= nil do
	local _, time = wait(0.1)
	move(time)

function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
	if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then
		for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do
			connection:disconnect()
		end
	end
	animTable[name] = {}
	animTable[name].count = 0
	animTable[name].totalWeight = 0	
	animTable[name].connections = {}

	-- check for config values
	local config = script:FindFirstChild(name)
	if (config ~= nil) then
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		local idx = 1
		for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do
			if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then
				table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
				animTable[name][idx] = {}
				animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart
				local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight")
				if (weightObject == nil) then
					animTable[name][idx].weight = 1
				else
					animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value
				end
				animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
				animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight
				idx = idx + 1
			end
		end
	end

	-- fallback to defaults
	if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then
		for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do
			animTable[name][idx] = {}
			animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation")
			animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name
			animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id
			animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight
			animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
			animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight
		end
	end
end

	if (fileList ~= nil) then
		configureAnimationSet(child.Name, fileList)
	end	
end

script.ChildAdded:connect(scriptChildModified)
script.ChildRemoved:connect(scriptChildModified)

for name, fileList in pairs(animNames) do 
	configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
end	

-- ANIMATION

-- declarations
local toolAnim = "None"
local toolAnimTime = 0

local jumpAnimTime = 0
local jumpAnimDuration = 0.3

local toolTransitionTime = 0.1
local fallTransitionTime = 0.3
local jumpMaxLimbVelocity = 0.75

-- functions

function stopAllAnimations()
	local oldAnim = currentAnim

	-- return to idle if finishing an emote
	if (emoteNames[oldAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[oldAnim] == false) then
		oldAnim = "idle"
	end

	currentAnim = ""
	currentAnimInstance = nil
	if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		currentAnimTrack:Stop()
		currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		currentAnimTrack = nil
	end
	return oldAnim
end

function setAnimationSpeed(speed)
	if speed ~= currentAnimSpeed then
		currentAnimSpeed = speed
		currentAnimTrack:AdjustSpeed(currentAnimSpeed)
	end
end

function keyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then

		local repeatAnim = currentAnim
		-- return to idle if finishing an emote
		if (emoteNames[repeatAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[repeatAnim] == false) then
			repeatAnim = "idle"
		end

		local animSpeed = currentAnimSpeed
		playAnimation(repeatAnim, 0.0, Humanoid)
		setAnimationSpeed(animSpeed)
	end
end

-- Preload animations
function playAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid) 
	-- Check if injured and override animation if needed
	local actualAnimName = animName
	if isInjured() then
		if animName == "idle" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredidle"
		elseif animName == "walk" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredwalk"
		elseif animName == "run" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredrun"
		end
	end

	if animTable[actualAnimName] == nil then
		-- Fallback to regular animation if injured version doesn't exist
		actualAnimName = animName
	end

	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[actualAnimName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[actualAnimName][idx].anim

	-- switch animation		
	if (anim ~= currentAnimInstance) then

		if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			currentAnimTrack:Stop(transitionTime)
			currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		end

		currentAnimSpeed = 1.0

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		currentAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		currentAnimTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Core

		-- play the animation
		currentAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		currentAnim = actualAnimName
		currentAnimInstance = anim

		-- set up keyframe name triggers
		if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
			currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
		end
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler = currentAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(keyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

local toolAnimName = ""
local toolAnimTrack = nil
local toolAnimInstance = nil
local currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = nil

function toolKeyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then
		playToolAnimation(toolAnimName, 0.0, Humanoid)
	end
end

function playToolAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid, priority)	 
	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[animName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[animName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[animName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[animName][idx].anim

	if (toolAnimInstance ~= anim) then
		if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			toolAnimTrack:Stop()
			toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
			transitionTime = 0
		end

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		toolAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		if priority then
			toolAnimTrack.Priority = priority
		end

		-- play the animation
		toolAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		toolAnimName = animName
		toolAnimInstance = anim

		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = toolAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(toolKeyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

function stopToolAnimations()
	local oldAnim = toolAnimName

	if (currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	toolAnimName = ""
	toolAnimInstance = nil
	if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		toolAnimTrack:Stop()
		toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
		toolAnimTrack = nil
	end

	return oldAnim
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function onRunning(speed)
	RunningSpeed = speed
	if speed > 0.01 then
		if speed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run", 0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
		if currentAnimInstance and (currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=180426354" or 
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=252557606" or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredwalk[1].id or
			currentAnimInstance.AnimationId == animNames.injuredrun[1].id) then
			if speed > 20 then
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 29.0)
			else
				setAnimationSpeed(speed / 14.5)
			end
		end
		pose = "Running"
	else
		if emoteNames[currentAnim] == nil then
			playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
			pose = "Standing"
		end
	end
end

function onDied()
	pose = "Dead"
end

function onJumping()
	playAnimation("jump", 0.1, Humanoid)
	jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimDuration
	pose = "Jumping"
end

function onClimbing(speed)
	playAnimation("climb", 0.1, Humanoid)
	setAnimationSpeed(speed / 12.0)
	pose = "Climbing"
end

function onGettingUp()
	pose = "GettingUp"
end

function onFreeFall()
	if (jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	end
	pose = "FreeFall"
end

function onFallingDown()
	pose = "FallingDown"
end

function onSeated()
	pose = "Seated"
end

function onPlatformStanding()
	pose = "PlatformStanding"
end

function onSwimming(speed)
	if speed > 0 then
		pose = "Running"
	else
		pose = "Standing"
	end
end

function getTool()	
	for _, kid in ipairs(Figure:GetChildren()) do
		if kid.className == "Tool" then return kid end
	end
	return nil
end

function getToolAnim(tool)
	for _, c in ipairs(tool:GetChildren()) do
		if c.Name == "toolanim" and c.className == "StringValue" then
			return c
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function animateTool()
	if (toolAnim == "None") then
		playToolAnimation("toolnone", toolTransitionTime, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Idle)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Slash") then
		playToolAnimation("toolslash", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end

	if (toolAnim == "Lunge") then
		playToolAnimation("toollunge", 0, Humanoid, Enum.AnimationPriority.Action)
		return
	end
end

function moveSit()
	RightShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	LeftShoulder.MaxVelocity = 0.15
	RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
	RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(3.14 /2)
	LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-3.14 /2)
end

local lastTick = 0

function move(time)
	local amplitude = 1
	local frequency = 1
	local deltaTime = time - lastTick
	lastTick = time

	local climbFudge = 0
	local setAngles = false

	if (jumpAnimTime > 0) then
		jumpAnimTime = jumpAnimTime - deltaTime
	end

	if (pose == "FreeFall" and jumpAnimTime <= 0) then
		playAnimation("fall", fallTransitionTime, Humanoid)
	elseif (pose == "Seated") then
		playAnimation("sit", 0.5, Humanoid)
		return
	elseif (pose == "Running") then
		if RunningSpeed > 20 then
			playAnimation("run",0.1, Humanoid)
		else
			playAnimation("walk", 0.1, Humanoid)
		end
	elseif (pose == "Dead" or pose == "GettingUp" or pose == "FallingDown" or pose == "Seated" or pose == "PlatformStanding") then
		stopAllAnimations()
		amplitude = 0.1
		frequency = 1
		setAngles = true
	end

	if (setAngles) then
		local desiredAngle = amplitude * math.sin(time * frequency)

		RightShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle + climbFudge)
		LeftShoulder:SetDesiredAngle(desiredAngle - climbFudge)
		RightHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
		LeftHip:SetDesiredAngle(-desiredAngle)
	end

	-- Tool Animation handling
	local tool = getTool()
	if tool and tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
		local animStringValueObject = getToolAnim(tool)

		if animStringValueObject then
			toolAnim = animStringValueObject.Value
			animStringValueObject.Parent = nil
			toolAnimTime = time + .3
		end

		if time > toolAnimTime then
			toolAnimTime = 0
			toolAnim = "None"
		end

		animateTool()		
	else
		stopToolAnimations()
		toolAnim = "None"
		toolAnimInstance = nil
		toolAnimTime = 0
	end
end

-- connect events
Humanoid.Died:connect(onDied)
Humanoid.Running:connect(onRunning)
Humanoid.Jumping:connect(onJumping)
Humanoid.Climbing:connect(onClimbing)
Humanoid.GettingUp:connect(onGettingUp)
Humanoid.FreeFalling:connect(onFreeFall)
Humanoid.FallingDown:connect(onFallingDown)
Humanoid.Seated:connect(onSeated)
Humanoid.PlatformStanding:connect(onPlatformStanding)
Humanoid.Swimming:connect(onSwimming)

-- setup emote chat hook
game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Chatted:connect(function(msg)
	local emote = ""
	if msg == "/e dance" then
		emote = dances[math.random(1, #dances)]
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 3) == "/e ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 4)
	elseif (string.sub(msg, 1, 7) == "/emote ") then
		emote = string.sub(msg, 8)
	end

	if (pose == "Standing" and emoteNames[emote] ~= nil) then
		playAnimation(emote, 0.1, Humanoid)
	end
end)

-- initialize to idle
playAnimation("idle", 0.1, Humanoid)
pose = "Standing"

while Figure.Parent ~= nil do
	local _, time = wait(0.1)
	move(time)

		end
		blockval:Destroy()

		humanoid.AutoRotate = true
		inputLock.Value = false
	end

local dances = {"dance1", "dance2", "dance3"}

-- Existance in this list signifies that it is an emote, the value indicates if it is a looping emote
local emoteNames = { wave = false, point = false, dance1 = true, dance2 = true, dance3 = true, laugh = false, cheer = false}

function isInjured()
	return Humanoid.Health < 50
end

function configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)
	if (animTable[name] ~= nil) then
		for _, connection in pairs(animTable[name].connections) do
			connection:disconnect()
		end
	end
	animTable[name] = {}
	animTable[name].count = 0
	animTable[name].totalWeight = 0	
	animTable[name].connections = {}

	-- check for config values
	local config = script:FindFirstChild(name)
	if (config ~= nil) then
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildAdded:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		table.insert(animTable[name].connections, config.ChildRemoved:connect(function(child) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
		local idx = 1
		for _, childPart in pairs(config:GetChildren()) do
			if (childPart:IsA("Animation")) then
				table.insert(animTable[name].connections, childPart.Changed:connect(function(property) configureAnimationSet(name, fileList) end))
				animTable[name][idx] = {}
				animTable[name][idx].anim = childPart
				local weightObject = childPart:FindFirstChild("Weight")
				if (weightObject == nil) then
					animTable[name][idx].weight = 1
				else
					animTable[name][idx].weight = weightObject.Value
				end
				animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
				animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + animTable[name][idx].weight
				idx = idx + 1
			end
		end
	end

	-- fallback to defaults
	if (animTable[name].count <= 0) then
		for idx, anim in pairs(fileList) do
			animTable[name][idx] = {}
			animTable[name][idx].anim = Instance.new("Animation")
			animTable[name][idx].anim.Name = name
			animTable[name][idx].anim.AnimationId = anim.id
			animTable[name][idx].weight = anim.weight
			animTable[name].count = animTable[name].count + 1
			animTable[name].totalWeight = animTable[name].totalWeight + anim.weight
		end
	end
end

-- Setup animation objects
function scriptChildModified(child)
	local fileList = animNames[child.Name]
	if (fileList ~= nil) then
		configureAnimationSet(child.Name, fileList)
	end	
end

script.ChildAdded:connect(scriptChildModified)
script.ChildRemoved:connect(scriptChildModified)

for name, fileList in pairs(animNames) do 
	configureAnimationSet(name, fileList)

-- ANIMATION

-- declarations
local toolAnim = "None"
local toolAnimTime = 0

local jumpAnimTime = 0
local jumpAnimDuration = 0.3

local toolTransitionTime = 0.1
local fallTransitionTime = 0.3
local jumpMaxLimbVelocity = 0.75

-- functions

function stopAllAnimations()
	local oldAnim = currentAnim

	-- return to idle if finishing an emote
	if (emoteNames[oldAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[oldAnim] == false) then
		oldAnim = "idle"
	end

	currentAnim = ""
	currentAnimInstance = nil
	if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		currentAnimTrack:Stop()
		currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		currentAnimTrack = nil
	end
	return oldAnim
end

function setAnimationSpeed(speed)
	if speed ~= currentAnimSpeed then
		currentAnimSpeed = speed
		currentAnimTrack:AdjustSpeed(currentAnimSpeed)
	end
end

function keyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then

		local repeatAnim = currentAnim
		-- return to idle if finishing an emote
		if (emoteNames[repeatAnim] ~= nil and emoteNames[repeatAnim] == false) then
			repeatAnim = "idle"
		end

		local animSpeed = currentAnimSpeed
		playAnimation(repeatAnim, 0.0, Humanoid)
		setAnimationSpeed(animSpeed)
	end
end

-- Preload animations
function playAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid) 
	-- Check if injured and override animation if needed
	local actualAnimName = animName
	if isInjured() then
		if animName == "idle" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredidle"
		elseif animName == "walk" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredwalk"
		elseif animName == "run" then
			actualAnimName = "injuredrun"
		end
	end

	if animTable[actualAnimName] == nil then
		-- Fallback to regular animation if injured version doesn't exist
		actualAnimName = animName
	end

	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[actualAnimName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[actualAnimName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[actualAnimName][idx].anim

	-- switch animation		
	if (anim ~= currentAnimInstance) then

		if (currentAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			currentAnimTrack:Stop(transitionTime)
			currentAnimTrack:Destroy()
		end

		currentAnimSpeed = 1.0

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		currentAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		currentAnimTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Core

		-- play the animation
		currentAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		currentAnim = actualAnimName
		currentAnimInstance = anim

		-- set up keyframe name triggers
		if (currentAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
			currentAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
		end
		currentAnimKeyframeHandler = currentAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(keyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

local toolAnimName = ""
local toolAnimTrack = nil
local toolAnimInstance = nil
local currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = nil

function toolKeyFrameReachedFunc(frameName)
	if (frameName == "End") then
		playToolAnimation(toolAnimName, 0.0, Humanoid)
	end
end

function playToolAnimation(animName, transitionTime, humanoid, priority)	 
	local roll = math.random(1, animTable[animName].totalWeight) 
	local origRoll = roll
	local idx = 1
	while (roll > animTable[animName][idx].weight) do
		roll = roll - animTable[animName][idx].weight
		idx = idx + 1
	end

	local anim = animTable[animName][idx].anim

	if (toolAnimInstance ~= anim) then
		if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
			toolAnimTrack:Stop()
			toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
			transitionTime = 0
		end

		-- load it to the humanoid; get AnimationTrack
		toolAnimTrack = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		if priority then
			toolAnimTrack.Priority = priority
		end

		-- play the animation
		toolAnimTrack:Play(transitionTime)
		toolAnimName = animName
		toolAnimInstance = anim

		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler = toolAnimTrack.KeyframeReached:connect(toolKeyFrameReachedFunc)
	end
end

function stopToolAnimations()
	local oldAnim = toolAnimName

	if (currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler ~= nil) then
		currentToolAnimKeyframeHandler:disconnect()
	end

	toolAnimName = ""
	toolAnimInstance = nil
	if (toolAnimTrack ~= nil) then
		toolAnimTrack:Stop()
		toolAnimTrack:Destroy()
		toolAnimTrack = nil
	end

	return oldAnim
end
