  21:59:23.098  --- Module : Maid ---  -  Edit
  21:59:23.098  Path: ReplicatedStorage.Modules.SmoothShiftLock.Maid  -  Edit
  21:59:23.099  ---------- Source ----------  -  Edit
  21:59:23.099  --[=[
	Manages the cleaning of events and other things. Useful for
	encapsulating state and make deconstructors easy.

	See the [Five Powerful Code Patterns talk](https://developer.roblox.com/en-us/videos/5-powerful-code-patterns-behind-top-roblox-games)
	for a more in-depth look at Maids in top games.

	```lua
	local maid = Maid.new()

	maid:GiveTask(function()
		print("Cleaning up")
	end)

	maid:GiveTask(workspace.ChildAdded:Connect(print))

	-- Disconnects all events, and executes all functions
	maid:DoCleaning()
	```

	@class Maid
]=]
-- luacheck: pop

local Maid = {}
Maid.ClassName = "Maid"

--[=[
	Constructs a new Maid object

	```lua
	local maid = Maid.new()
	```

	@return Maid
]=]
function Maid.new()
	return setmetatable({
		_tasks = {}
	}, Maid)
end

--[=[
	Returns true if the class is a maid, and false otherwise.

	```lua
	print(Maid.isMaid(Maid.new())) --> true
	print(Maid.isMaid(nil)) --> false
	```

	@param value any
	@return boolean
]=]
function Maid.isMaid(value)
	return type(value) == "table" and value.ClassName == "Maid"
end

--[=[
	Returns Maid[key] if not part of Maid metatable

	```lua
	local maid = Maid.new()
	maid._current = Instance.new("Part")
	print(maid._current) --> Part

	maid._current = nil
	print(maid._current) --> nil
	```

	@param index any
	@return MaidTask
]=]
function Maid:__index(index)
	if Maid[index] then
		return Maid[index]
	else
		return self._tasks[index]
	end
end

--[=[
	Add a task to clean up. Tasks given to a maid will be cleaned when
	maid[index] is set to a different value.

	Task cleanup is such that if the task is an event, it is disconnected.
	If it is an object, it is destroyed.

	```
	Maid[key] = (function)         Adds a task to perform
	Maid[key] = (event connection) Manages an event connection
	Maid[key] = (thread)           Manages a thread
	Maid[key] = (Maid)             Maids can act as an event connection, allowing a Maid to have other maids to clean up.
	Maid[key] = (Object)           Maids can cleanup objects with a `Destroy` method
	Maid[key] = nil                Removes a named task.
	```

	@param index any
	@param newTask MaidTask
]=]
function Maid:__newindex(index, newTask)
	if Maid[index] ~= nil then
		error(("Cannot use '%s' as a Maid key"):format(tostring(index)), 2)
	end

	local tasks = self._tasks
	local oldTask = tasks[index]

	if oldTask == newTask then
		return
	end

	tasks[index] = newTask

	if oldTask then
		if type(oldTask) == "function" then
			oldTask()
		elseif type(oldTask) == "thread" then
			task.cancel(oldTask)
		elseif typeof(oldTask) == "RBXScriptConnection" then
			oldTask:Disconnect()
		elseif oldTask.Destroy then
			oldTask:Destroy()
		end
	end
end

--[=[
	Gives a task to the maid for cleanup, but uses an incremented number as a key.

	@param task MaidTask -- An item to clean
	@return number -- taskId
]=]
function Maid:GiveTask(task)
	if not task then
		error("Task cannot be false or nil", 2)
	end

	local taskId = #self._tasks+1
	self[taskId] = task

	if type(task) == "table" and (not task.Destroy) then
		warn("[Maid.GiveTask] - Gave table task without .Destroy\n\n" .. debug.traceback())
	end

	return taskId
end

--[=[
	Gives a promise to the maid for clean.

	@param promise Promise<T>
	@return Promise<T>
]=]
function Maid:GivePromise(promise)
	if not promise:IsPending() then
		return promise
	end

	local newPromise = promise.resolved(promise)
	local id = self:GiveTask(newPromise)

	-- Ensure GC
	newPromise:Finally(function()
		self[id] = nil
	end)

	return newPromise
end

--[=[
	Cleans up all tasks and removes them as entries from the Maid.

	:::note
	Signals that are already connected are always disconnected first. After that
	any signals added during a cleaning phase will be disconnected at random times.
	:::

	:::tip
	DoCleaning() may be recursively invoked. This allows the you to ensure that
	tasks or other tasks. Each task will be executed once.

	However, adding tasks while cleaning is not generally a good idea, as if you add a
	function that adds itself, this will loop indefinitely.
	:::
]=]
function Maid:DoCleaning()
	local tasks = self._tasks

	-- Disconnect all events first as we know this is safe
	for index, job in pairs(tasks) do
		if typeof(job) == "RBXScriptConnection" then
			tasks[index] = nil
			job:Disconnect()
		end
	end

	-- Clear out tasks table completely, even if clean up tasks add more tasks to the maid
	local index, job = next(tasks)
	while job ~= nil do
		tasks[index] = nil
		if type(job) == "function" then
			job()
		elseif type(job) == "thread" then
			task.cancel(job)
		elseif typeof(job) == "RBXScriptConnection" then
			job:Disconnect()
		elseif job.Destroy then
			job:Destroy()
		end
		index, job = next(tasks)
	end
end

--[=[
	Alias for [Maid.DoCleaning()](/api/Maid#DoCleaning)

	@function Destroy
	@within Maid
]=]
Maid.Destroy = Maid.DoCleaning

return Maid

  21:59:23.099  --- Module : Spring ---  -  Edit
  21:59:23.099  Path: ReplicatedStorage.Modules.SmoothShiftLock.Spring  -  Edit
  21:59:23.099  ---------- Source ----------  -  Edit
  21:59:23.099  --[=[
	A physical model of a spring, useful in many applications.
	A spring is an object that will compute based upon Hooke's law. Properties only evaluate
	upon index making this model good for lazy applications.
	```lua
	local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local spring = Spring.new(Vector3.new(0, 0, 0))
	RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then
			spring.Target = Vector3.new(0, 0, 1)
		else
			spring.Target = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		end
		print(spring.Position) -- A smoothed out version of the input keycode W
	end)
	```
	A good visualization can be found here, provided by Defaultio:
	https://www.desmos.com/calculator/hn2i9shxbz
	@class Spring
]=]
local Spring = {}

--[=[
	Constructs a new Spring at the position and target specified, of type T.
	```lua
	-- Linear spring
	local linearSpring = Spring.new(0)
	-- Vector2 spring
	local vector2Spring = Spring.new(Vector2.new(0, 0))
	-- Vector3 spring
	local vector3Spring = Spring.new(Vector3.new(0, 0, 0))
	```
	@param initial T -- The initial parameter is a number or Vector3 (anything with * number and addition/subtraction).
	@param clock? () -> number -- The clock function is optional, and is used to update the spring
	@return Spring<T>
]=]
function Spring.new(initial, clock)
	local target = initial or 0
	clock = clock or os.clock
	return setmetatable({
		_clock = clock;
		_time0 = clock();
		_position0 = target;
		_velocity0 = 0*target;
		_target = target;
		_damper = 1;
		_speed = 1;
	}, Spring)
end

--[=[
	Impulses the spring, increasing velocity by the amount given. This is useful to make something shake,
	like a Mac password box failing.
	@param velocity T -- The velocity to impulse with
	@return ()
]=]
function Spring:Impulse(velocity)
	self.Velocity = self.Velocity + velocity
end

--[=[
	Instantly skips the spring forwards by that amount time
	@param delta number -- Time to skip forwards
	@return ()
]=]
function Spring:TimeSkip(delta)
	local now = self._clock()
	local position, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(now+delta)
	self._position0 = position
	self._velocity0 = velocity
	self._time0 = now
end

--[=[
	The current position at the given clock time. Assigning the position will change the spring to have that position.
	```lua
	local spring = Spring.new(0)
	print(spring.Position) --> 0
	```
	@prop Position T
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	Alias for [Spring.Position](/api/Spring#Position)
	@prop p T
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	The current velocity. Assigning the velocity will change the spring to have that velocity.
	```lua
	local spring = Spring.new(0)
	print(spring.Velocity) --> 0
	```
	@prop Velocity T
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	Alias for [Spring.Velocity](/api/Spring#Velocity)
	@prop v T
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	The current target. Assigning the target will change the spring to have that target.
	```lua
	local spring = Spring.new(0)
	print(spring.Target) --> 0
	```
	@prop Target T
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	Alias for [Spring.Target](/api/Spring#Target)
	@prop t T
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	The current damper, defaults to 1. At 1 the spring is critically damped. At less than 1, it
	will be underdamped, and thus, bounce, and at over 1, it will be critically damped.
	@prop Damper number
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	Alias for [Spring.Damper](/api/Spring#Damper)
	@prop d number
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	The speed, defaults to 1, but should be between [0, infinity)
	@prop Speed number
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	Alias for [Spring.Speed](/api/Spring#Speed)
	@prop s number
	@within Spring
]=]
--[=[
	The current clock object to syncronize the spring against.
	@prop Clock () -> number
	@within Spring
]=]
function Spring:__index(index)
	if Spring[index] then
		return Spring[index]
	elseif index == "Value" or index == "Position" or index == "p" then
		local position, _ = self:_positionVelocity(self._clock())
		return position
	elseif index == "Velocity" or index == "v" then
		local _, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(self._clock())
		return velocity
	elseif index == "Target" or index == "t" then
		return self._target
	elseif index == "Damper" or index == "d" then
		return self._damper
	elseif index == "Speed" or index == "s" then
		return self._speed
	elseif index == "Clock" then
		return self._clock
	else
		error(("%q is not a valid member of Spring"):format(tostring(index)), 2)
	end
end

function Spring:__newindex(index, value)
	local now = self._clock()

	if index == "Value" or index == "Position" or index == "p" then
		local _, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(now)
		self._position0 = value
		self._velocity0 = velocity
		self._time0 = now
	elseif index == "Velocity" or index == "v" then
		local position, _ = self:_positionVelocity(now)
		self._position0 = position
		self._velocity0 = value
		self._time0 = now
	elseif index == "Target" or index == "t" then
		local position, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(now)
		self._position0 = position
		self._velocity0 = velocity
		self._target = value
		self._time0 = now
	elseif index == "Damper" or index == "d" then
		local position, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(now)
		self._position0 = position
		self._velocity0 = velocity
		self._damper = value
		self._time0 = now
	elseif index == "Speed" or index == "s" then
		local position, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(now)
		self._position0 = position
		self._velocity0 = velocity
		self._speed = value < 0 and 0 or value
		self._time0 = now
	elseif index == "Clock" then
		local position, velocity = self:_positionVelocity(now)
		self._position0 = position
		self._velocity0 = velocity
		self._clock = value
		self._time0 = value()
	else
		error(("%q is not a valid member of Spring"):format(tostring(index)), 2)
	end
end

function Spring:_positionVelocity(now)
	local p0 = self._position0
	local v0 = self._velocity0
	local p1 = self._target
	local d = self._damper
	local s = self._speed

	local t = s*(now - self._time0)
	local d2 = d*d

	local h, si, co
	if d2 < 1 then
		h = math.sqrt(1 - d2)
		local ep = math.exp(-d*t)/h
		co, si = ep*math.cos(h*t), ep*math.sin(h*t)
	elseif d2 == 1 then
		h = 1
		local ep = math.exp(-d*t)/h
		co, si = ep, ep*t
	else
		h = math.sqrt(d2 - 1)
		local u = math.exp((-d + h)*t)/(2*h)
		local v = math.exp((-d - h)*t)/(2*h)
		co, si = u + v, u - v
	end

	local a0 = h*co + d*si
	local a1 = 1 - (h*co + d*si)
	local a2 = si/s

	local b0 = -s*si
	local b1 = s*si
	local b2 = h*co - d*si

	return
		a0*p0 + a1*p1 + a2*v0,
		b0*p0 + b1*p1 + b2*v0
end

-- This function produces a folder under a specified parent.
-- "soundProperties" is a table determining what the default properties of these audios will be.
function main:CreateSoundGroup(parent:Instance?, name:string?, soundProperties:{}?, isFolder:boolean?) : SoundGroup|Folder
	if not parent then warn("Parent not specified, Footstep folder parented to workspace") end
	isFolder = isFolder or false
	soundProperties = soundProperties or {}
	parent = parent or workspace
	-- Create folder
	local SoundGroup = nil
	if not isFolder then
		SoundGroup = Instance.new("SoundGroup"); SoundGroup.Volume = 1; SoundGroup.Name = name or "Footsteps"
	else
		SoundGroup = Instance.new("Folder"); SoundGroup.Name = name or "Footsteps"
	end
	local index = 0
	for soundMaterial,soundList in pairs(main.SoundIds) do
		index = 0
		local sectionGroup = nil
		if not isFolder then
			sectionGroup = Instance.new("SoundGroup"); sectionGroup.Volume = 1; sectionGroup.Name = soundMaterial
		else
			sectionGroup = Instance.new("Folder"); sectionGroup.Name = soundMaterial
		end
		for _,soundId in pairs(soundList) do
			index += 1 -- Increment index
			local soundEffect = Instance.new("Sound")
			soundEffect.Name = string.format("%s_%02i",soundMaterial:lower(),index)
			-- Set optional sound group
			if not isFolder then
				soundEffect.SoundGroup = sectionGroup
			end
			for property,value in pairs(soundProperties) do
				soundEffect[property] = value
			end
			soundEffect.SoundId = soundId
			soundEffect.Parent = sectionGroup
		end
		sectionGroup.Parent = SoundGroup
	end
	
	SoundGroup.Parent = parent
	return SoundGroup
end

-- This function returns a table from the MaterialMap given the material.
function main:GetTableFromMaterial(EnumItem : Enum.Material|string) : {}
	if typeof(EnumItem) == "string" then -- CONVERSION
		EnumItem = Enum.Material[EnumItem]
	end
	return main.MaterialMap[EnumItem]
end

-- This function is a primitive "pick randomly from table" function.
function main:GetRandomSound(SoundTable : {}) : string
	return SoundTable[math.random(#SoundTable)]
end

  21:59:23.103  local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local SoundService = game:GetService("SoundService")

local Round = require(script:WaitForChild("RoundModule"))
local Characters = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Characters")
local Cutscenes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Cutscenes")
local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local Values = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Values")

local TimerValue = Values:WaitForChild("TimerValue")
local StatusValue = Values:WaitForChild("StatusValue")

local MIN_PLAYERS = 1

local function getAvailablePlayers()
	local available = {}
	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		local inShop = plr:FindFirstChild("InShop")
		if not inShop or inShop.Value == false then
			table.insert(available, plr)
		end
	end
	return available
end

local function getPlayerCount()
	return #getAvailablePlayers()
end

while true do
	repeat
		local playerCount = getPlayerCount()
		StatusValue.Value = "Waiting for more players..."
		TimerValue.Value = string.format("(%d/%d)", playerCount, MIN_PLAYERS)
		task.wait(1)
	until playerCount >= MIN_PLAYERS

	Round.Intermission(30)

	local survivors = getAvailablePlayers()
	
	if #survivors == 0 then
		continue
	end

	local chosenKiller = Round.ChooseKiller(survivors)

	if not chosenKiller then
		warn("No killer chosen, returning to intermission.")
		continue
	end

	local killerIndex = table.find(survivors, chosenKiller)
	if killerIndex then
		table.remove(survivors, killerIndex)
	end

	if #survivors == 0 then
		warn("No survivors left after choosing killer, returning to intermission.")
		continue
	end

	local chosenMap = Round.ChooseMap()
	local newMap = chosenMap:Clone()
	newMap.Parent = workspace
	newMap.Name = "Map"

	StatusValue.Value = chosenMap.Name .. " has been chosen."
	task.wait(5)

	local playerData = chosenKiller:WaitForChild("PlayerData")
	local killerName = playerData:WaitForChild("EquippedKiller").Value
	local killerSkin = playerData:WaitForChild("Killers"):WaitForChild(killerName):WaitForChild("EquippedSkin").Value

	local killerCharacter = Characters:WaitForChild("Killers"):WaitForChild(killerName):WaitForChild(killerSkin):Clone()
	local introCutscene = Cutscenes:WaitForChild(killerName):Clone()
	introCutscene.Parent = workspace

	killerCharacter.Name = "Character"
	killerCharacter.Parent = introCutscene
	killerCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart").Anchored = true
	killerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = introCutscene.Spawn.CFrame

	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		plr.InCutscene.Value = true
	end

	Remotes.TransitionEvent:FireAllClients(0.3, 50, 0.4)
	Remotes.LightingEvent:FireClient(chosenKiller, killerName)
	for _, survivor in ipairs(survivors) do
		Remotes.LightingEvent:FireClient(survivor, killerName)
	end
	task.wait(0.4)
	Remotes.IntroRemote:FireAllClients(introCutscene, killerName, chosenKiller.Name)

	task.wait(introCutscene.CutsceneDuration.Value)
	Remotes.TransitionEvent:FireAllClients(0.5, 50, 1)
	task.wait(0.9)

	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		plr.InCutscene.Value = false
	end

	Remotes.LightingEvent:FireClient(chosenKiller, chosenMap.Name)
	for _, survivor in ipairs(survivors) do
		Remotes.LightingEvent:FireClient(survivor, chosenMap.Name)
	end
	
	Round.InsertTag(survivors, "Survivor")
	Round.InsertTag({ chosenKiller }, "Killer")

	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if plr:FindFirstChild("Killer") or plr:FindFirstChild("Survivor") then
			Round.ApplyCharacter(plr)

			local char = plr.Character or plr.CharacterAdded:Wait()
			local hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

			hum.Died:Connect(function()
				Remotes.LightingEvent:FireClient(plr, "Lobby")
			end)
		end
	end


	Round.TeleportSurvivors(survivors, chosenMap.SurvivorSpawns:GetChildren())
	Round.TeleportKiller(chosenKiller, chosenMap.KillerSpawn:GetChildren())

	Round.Round(210)
	
	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if table.find(survivors, plr) then
			local plrData = plr:WaitForChild("PlayerData")
			plrData.Hatred.Value += 1
		end
	end
	
	
	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		Remotes.CharacterChanged:FireClient(plr, nil, nil)
	end

	task.wait(5)
	Remotes.TransitionEvent:FireAllClients(1, 50, 1)
	SoundService.LastManStanding:Stop()

	task.wait(1)
	Values.LastManStanding.Value = false

	for _, plr in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if not plr.Character then
			Remotes.CharacterChanged:FireClient(plr, nil, nil)
			plr.InputLocked.Value = false
			plr:LoadCharacterAsync()
		end
	end

	Round.RemoveTags()
	newMap:Destroy()
	introCutscene:Destroy()
	table.clear(survivors)
	workspace.Debris:ClearAllChildren()

	Remotes.LightingEvent:FireAllClients("Lobby")
end

  21:59:23.104  local module = {}

local SoundService = game:GetService("SoundService")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local Values = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Values")

local TimerValue = Values:WaitForChild("TimerValue")
local StatusValue = Values:WaitForChild("StatusValue")
local LastManStanding = Values:WaitForChild("LastManStanding")

local CharacterChanged = Remotes:WaitForChild("CharacterChanged")
local lastChosenMap

local function toMS(s)
	return ("%d:%02i"):format(s/60%60, s%60)
end


local function fadeSound(sound, targetVolume, duration)
	local tween = TweenService:Create(sound, TweenInfo.new(duration, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear), {Volume = targetVolume})
	tween:Play()
	return tween
end

local function playWithFadeIn(sound, duration)
	sound.Volume = 0
	sound:Play()
	fadeSound(sound, sound:GetAttribute("DefaultVolume") or 1, duration)
end

local function stopWithFadeOut(sound, duration)
	local tween = fadeSound(sound, 0, duration)
	tween.Completed:Connect(function()
		sound:Stop()
	end)
end


function module.ChooseKiller(players)
	local validPlayers = {}

	for _, player in ipairs(players) do
		local inShop = player:FindFirstChild("InShop")
		if (not inShop or not inShop.Value)
			and player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
			and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Hatred") then
			table.insert(validPlayers, player)
		end
	end

	if #validPlayers == 0 then
		warn("No valid players to choose as killer.")
		return nil
	end

	local highestHatred = -math.huge
	local topPlayers = {}

	for _, player in ipairs(validPlayers) do
		local hatred = player.leaderstats.Hatred.Value

		if hatred > highestHatred then
			highestHatred = hatred
			topPlayers = { player }
		elseif hatred == highestHatred then
			table.insert(topPlayers, player)
		end
	end

	local chosenKiller = topPlayers[math.random(1, #topPlayers)]
	chosenKiller.leaderstats.Hatred.Value = 1

	return chosenKiller
end



function module.InsertTag(contestants,tagName)
	for i, player in pairs(contestants) do
		local Tag = Instance.new("StringValue")
		Tag.Name = tagName
		Tag.Parent = player
	end
end

function module.Intermission(length)
	StatusValue.Value = "Intermission"
	for i = length,0,-1 do
		TimerValue.Value = toMS(i)
		task.wait(1)
	end
end

function module.Round(length)
	local timeleft = length
	local lastManMode = false
	StatusValue.Value = "Round in Progress"

	local escapedPlayers = {}
	local killerActive = true

	local function onHumanoidDied(player)
		if player:FindFirstChild("Survivor") then
			player.Survivor:Destroy()
			if not lastManMode then
				timeleft += 10
			end
		elseif player:FindFirstChild("Killer") then
			player.Killer:Destroy()
			killerActive = false
		end

		player.InputLocked.Value = false
		CharacterChanged:FireClient(player, nil, nil)
	end

	for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
			player.Character.Humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
				onHumanoidDied(player)
			end)
		end
	end

	while timeleft > 0 do
		local survivors = {}
		killerActive = false

		for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				local hum = player.Character.Humanoid
				if player:FindFirstChild("Survivor") and hum.Health > 0 then
					table.insert(survivors, player)
				elseif player:FindFirstChild("Killer") and hum.Health > 0 then
					killerActive = true
				end
			end
		end

		if not killerActive then
			StatusValue.Value = "The Killer has left or died. Survivors win!"
			return
		end

		if #survivors == 0 then
			StatusValue.Value = "The Killer has won the round."
			return
		elseif #survivors == 1 and not lastManMode then
			lastManMode = true
			timeleft = 88
			StatusValue.Value = "Final survivor remaining."
			LastManStanding.Value = true
			playWithFadeIn(SoundService.LastManStanding, 1)
		end

		TimerValue.Value = toMS(timeleft)
		timeleft -= 1
		task.wait(1)
	end

	
	stopWithFadeOut(SoundService.LastManStanding, 1)

	local survivorsLeft = {}
	local killerStillAlive = false

	for _, p in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if p:FindFirstChild("Survivor") then
			table.insert(survivorsLeft, p)
		elseif p:FindFirstChild("Killer") and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
			killerStillAlive = true
		end
	end

	if not killerStillAlive then
		StatusValue.Value = "The Killer has died. Survivors win!"
	elseif #survivorsLeft > 0 then
		StatusValue.Value = "Time’s up! Survivors Win!"
	else
		StatusValue.Value = "All Survivors eliminated. The Killer wins."
	end
end

function module.ChooseMap()
	local maps = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Maps"):GetChildren()

	if #maps == 0 then
		warn("No maps found in ReplicatedStorage.Maps.")
		return nil
	end

	if #maps == 1 then
		return maps[1]
	end

	local newMap
	repeat
		newMap = maps[math.random(1, #maps)]
	until newMap ~= lastChosenMap

	lastChosenMap = newMap
	return newMap
end


function module.RemoveTags()
	for i, v in pairs(game.Players:GetChildren()) do
		if v:FindFirstChild("Killer") then
			v.Killer:Destroy()
			v:LoadCharacter()
		elseif v:FindFirstChild("Survivor") then
			v.Survivor:Destroy()
			v:LoadCharacter()
		end
		CharacterChanged:FireClient(v,nil, nil)

	end

end

function module.TeleportSurvivors(players, survivorSpawns)

	for i, player in pairs(players) do
		if player.Character then
			local character = player.Character

			if character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				local rand = Random.new()
				player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = survivorSpawns[rand:NextInteger(1, #survivorSpawns)].CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
			end
		end
	end
end

function module.TeleportKiller(player, killerSpawn)

	if player.Character then
		local character = player.Character

		if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
			player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = killerSpawn[1].CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
		end
	end
end


function module.ApplyCharacter(plr)
	local dataFolder = plr:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
	if not dataFolder then
		warn("No PlayerData found for", plr.Name)
		return
	end

	local character
	local Killers = dataFolder:FindFirstChild("Killers")
	local Survivors = dataFolder:FindFirstChild("Survivors")

	local equippedKiller = dataFolder:FindFirstChild("EquippedKiller")
	local equippedSurvivor = dataFolder:FindFirstChild("EquippedSurvivor")

	local oldChar = plr.Character 

	if plr:FindFirstChild("Killer") then
		local killerName = equippedKiller and equippedKiller.Value or "user_004"
		local dataKiller = Killers:FindFirstChild(equippedKiller.Value)
		local killerFolder = game.ReplicatedStorage.Characters.Killers:FindFirstChild(killerName)

		if killerFolder and killerFolder:FindFirstChild("Default") then
			local skin = killerFolder:FindFirstChild(dataKiller.EquippedSkin.Value)
			character = skin:Clone()
			CharacterChanged:FireClient(plr, "Killer", killerName)

			local Theme = skin:WaitForChild("Theme")
			SoundService.ChaseTheme.SoundId = Theme:WaitForChild("Chase").Value
			SoundService.TerrorRadius1.SoundId = Theme:WaitForChild("Chase1").Value
			SoundService.TerrorRadius2.SoundId = Theme:WaitForChild("Chase2").Value

			local walkSpeedValue = killerFolder:FindFirstChild("WalkSpeed")
			task.defer(function()
				local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
				humanoid.WalkSpeed = walkSpeedValue.Value
			end)
		else
			warn("Killer not found:", killerName)
			return
		end

	elseif plr:FindFirstChild("Survivor") then
		local survivorName = equippedSurvivor and equippedSurvivor.Value or "Dummy"
		local dataSurvivor = Survivors:FindFirstChild(equippedSurvivor.Value)
		local survivorFolder = game.ReplicatedStorage.Characters.Survivors:FindFirstChild(survivorName)

		if survivorFolder and survivorFolder:FindFirstChild("Default") then
			local skin = survivorFolder:FindFirstChild(dataSurvivor.EquippedSkin.Value)
			character = skin:Clone()
			CharacterChanged:FireClient(plr, "Survivor", survivorName)

			local walkSpeedValue = survivorFolder:FindFirstChild("WalkSpeed")
			task.defer(function()
				local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
				humanoid.WalkSpeed = walkSpeedValue.Value
			end)
		else
			warn("Survivor not found:", survivorName)
			return
		end
	else
		warn("Player has no role assigned:", plr.Name)
		return
	end

	if oldChar and oldChar ~= character then
		for _, descendant in ipairs(oldChar:GetDescendants()) do
			if (descendant:IsA("Script") or descendant:IsA("LocalScript")) and descendant.Name ~= "Animate" then
				local clonedScript = descendant:Clone()
				clonedScript.Disabled = descendant.Disabled
				clonedScript.Parent = character
			end
		end
	end

	-- Apply character
	character.Name = plr.Name
	plr.Character = character
	character.Parent = workspace
end





return module

local cooldowns = {}

AbilityEvent.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, classType, charName, abilityName)
	local abilityList = CharacterModule.GetAbilities(classType, charName)
	if not abilityList then return end
print("Works")
	local chosenAbility
	for _, entry in ipairs(abilityList) do
		if entry.Name == abilityName then
			local abilityModule = CharacterModule.GetAbilityModule(classType, charName)
			chosenAbility = abilityModule[abilityName]
			break
		end
	end

	if not chosenAbility then
		warn("Invalid ability request from " .. player.Name .. " (" .. tostring(abilityName) .. ")")
		return
	end

	local inputLocked = player:FindFirstChild("InputLocked")
	if inputLocked and inputLocked.Value then
		return
	end

	cooldowns[player] = cooldowns[player] or {}
	local now = tick()
	local lastUsed = cooldowns[player][abilityName] or 0

	if chosenAbility.Cooldown and now - lastUsed < chosenAbility.Cooldown then
		return
	end

	if chosenAbility.Action then
		chosenAbility.Action(player)
	end

	cooldowns[player][abilityName] = now
end)

  21:59:23.107  local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local PlayerDataStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("newDataStore111")

local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local ShopEvent = Remotes:WaitForChild("ShopEvent")
local EquipEvent = Remotes:WaitForChild("EquipEvent")

local defaultKiller = "user_004"
local defaultSurvivor = "Dummy"
local defaultSkin = "Default"

local function createCharacterFolder(parentFolder, charName, equippedSkinName)
	local charFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
	charFolder.Name = charName
	charFolder.Parent = parentFolder

	local skinsFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
	skinsFolder.Name = "Skins"
	skinsFolder.Parent = charFolder

	local equippedSkin = Instance.new("StringValue")
	equippedSkin.Name = "EquippedSkin"
	equippedSkin.Value = equippedSkinName or defaultSkin
	equippedSkin.Parent = charFolder

	return charFolder
end

local function ensureDefaultSkin(charFolder)
	local skins = charFolder:FindFirstChild("Skins")
	if not skins then return end

	if #skins:GetChildren() == 0 then
		local b = Instance.new("BoolValue")
		b.Name = defaultSkin
		b.Value = true
		b.Parent = skins
	end
end

local function getKeyForPlayer(player)
	if RunService:IsStudio() then
		return "Studio_" .. game.JobId .. "_" .. player.Name
	else
		return tostring(player.UserId)
	end
end

local function loadPlayerData(player)
	local dataFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
	dataFolder.Name = "PlayerData"
	dataFolder.Parent = player

	local killersFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
	killersFolder.Name = "Killers"
	killersFolder.Parent = dataFolder

	local survivorsFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
	survivorsFolder.Name = "Survivors"
	survivorsFolder.Parent = dataFolder

	local equippedKiller = Instance.new("StringValue")
	equippedKiller.Name = "EquippedKiller"
	equippedKiller.Parent = dataFolder

	local equippedSurvivor = Instance.new("StringValue")
	equippedSurvivor.Name = "EquippedSurvivor"
	equippedSurvivor.Parent = dataFolder

	local tix = Instance.new("IntValue")
	tix.Name = "Tix"
	tix.Parent = dataFolder

	local hatred = Instance.new("IntValue")
	hatred.Name = "Hatred"
	hatred.Parent = dataFolder

	local key = getKeyForPlayer(player)
	local success, data = pcall(function()
		return PlayerDataStore:GetAsync(key)
	end)

	if not success or not data then
		tix.Value = 500
		hatred.Value = 1
		equippedKiller.Value = defaultKiller
		equippedSurvivor.Value = defaultSurvivor

		local k = createCharacterFolder(killersFolder, defaultKiller, defaultSkin)
		local s = createCharacterFolder(survivorsFolder, defaultSurvivor, defaultSkin)
		ensureDefaultSkin(k)
		ensureDefaultSkin(s)
		return
	end

	tix.Value = data.Tix or 500
	hatred.Value = data.Hatred or 1
	equippedKiller.Value = data.EquippedKiller or defaultKiller
	equippedSurvivor.Value = data.EquippedSurvivor or defaultSurvivor

	for _, k in ipairs(data.Killers or {}) do
		local char = createCharacterFolder(killersFolder, k.Name, k.EquippedSkin)
		for _, sname in ipairs(k.Skins or {}) do
			if not char.Skins:FindFirstChild(sname) then
				local b = Instance.new("BoolValue")
				b.Name = sname
				b.Value = true
				b.Parent = char.Skins
			end
		end
		char.EquippedSkin.Value = k.EquippedSkin or defaultSkin
		ensureDefaultSkin(char)
	end

	for _, s in ipairs(data.Survivors or {}) do
		local char = createCharacterFolder(survivorsFolder, s.Name, s.EquippedSkin)
		for _, sname in ipairs(s.Skins or {}) do
			if not char.Skins:FindFirstChild(sname) then
				local b = Instance.new("BoolValue")
				b.Name = sname
				b.Value = true
				b.Parent = char.Skins
			end
		end
		char.EquippedSkin.Value = s.EquippedSkin or defaultSkin
		ensureDefaultSkin(char)
	end
end

local saveCooldown = {}

local function savePlayerData(player, force)
	local dataFolder = player:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
	if not dataFolder then return end

	if not force then
		if saveCooldown[player] then return end
		saveCooldown[player] = true
		task.delay(3, function() saveCooldown[player] = nil end)
	end

	local killersData = {}
	for _, char in ipairs(dataFolder.Killers:GetChildren()) do
		local skins = {}
		local seen = {}

		for _, s in ipairs(char.Skins:GetChildren()) do
			if not seen[s.Name] then
				seen[s.Name] = true
				table.insert(skins, s.Name)
			end
		end

		table.insert(killersData, {
			Name = char.Name,
			EquippedSkin = char.EquippedSkin.Value,
			Skins = skins
		})
	end

	local survivorsData = {}
	for _, char in ipairs(dataFolder.Survivors:GetChildren()) do
		local skins = {}
		local seen = {}

		for _, s in ipairs(char.Skins:GetChildren()) do
			if not seen[s.Name] then
				seen[s.Name] = true
				table.insert(skins, s.Name)
			end
		end

		table.insert(survivorsData, {
			Name = char.Name,
			EquippedSkin = char.EquippedSkin.Value,
			Skins = skins
		})
	end

	local dataToSave = {
		Tix = dataFolder.Tix.Value,
		Hatred = dataFolder.Hatred.Value,
		EquippedKiller = dataFolder.EquippedKiller.Value,
		EquippedSurvivor = dataFolder.EquippedSurvivor.Value,
		Killers = killersData,
		Survivors = survivorsData
	}

	local key = getKeyForPlayer(player)

	pcall(function()
		PlayerDataStore:UpdateAsync(key, function(old)
			old = old or {}
			for k, v in pairs(dataToSave) do
				old[k] = v
			end
			return old
		end)
	end)
end

ShopEvent.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, itemData, category)
	if not itemData or not category then return end
	local dataFolder = player:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
	if not dataFolder then return end

	local tix = dataFolder:FindFirstChild("Tix")
	if not tix then return end

	if category == "Killers" or category == "Survivors" then
		local categoryFolder = dataFolder[category]
		local equippedValue = category == "Killers" and dataFolder.EquippedKiller or dataFolder.EquippedSurvivor
		local itemName = (type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.Name or itemData.ItemName)) or tostring(itemData)
		if not itemName then return end

		local ownedChar = categoryFolder:FindFirstChild(itemName)
		if ownedChar then
			equippedValue.Value = itemName
			EquipEvent:FireClient(player, itemName, category)
		else
			local cost = (type(itemData) == "table" and itemData.Cost) or 0
			if tix.Value >= cost then
				tix.Value -= cost
				local char = createCharacterFolder(categoryFolder, itemName, defaultSkin)
				ensureDefaultSkin(char)
				equippedValue.Value = itemName
				EquipEvent:FireClient(player, itemName, category)
				savePlayerData(player)
			else
				EquipEvent:FireClient(player, "NotEnoughTix", category)
			end
		end
		return
	end

	if category == "Skins" then
		local characterName = itemData.Character or itemData.Parent or itemData.ParentChar
		local skinName = itemData.Name or itemData.SkinName
		if not characterName or not skinName then return end

		local charFolder =
			dataFolder.Killers:FindFirstChild(characterName)
			or dataFolder.Survivors:FindFirstChild(characterName)

		if not charFolder then return end
		local skinsFolder = charFolder.Skins

		if skinsFolder:FindFirstChild(skinName) then
			charFolder.EquippedSkin.Value = skinName
			EquipEvent:FireClient(player, skinName, "Skins", characterName)
		else
			local cost = itemData.Cost or 0
			if tix.Value >= cost then
				tix.Value -= cost
				local b = Instance.new("BoolValue")
				b.Name = skinName
				b.Value = true
				b.Parent = skinsFolder
				charFolder.EquippedSkin.Value = skinName
				EquipEvent:FireClient(player, skinName, "Skins", characterName)
				savePlayerData(player)
			else
				EquipEvent:FireClient(player, "NotEnoughTix", "Skins", characterName)
			end
		end
	end
end)

Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(loadPlayerData)
Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(p)
	savePlayerData(p, true)
end)

game:BindToClose(function()
	for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		savePlayerData(p, true)
	end

  21:59:23.108  Path: ServerScriptService.FootstepsHandler  -  Edit

-- // Services
local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local playersService = game:GetService("Players")

-- // Variables
local Modules = replicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Modules")
local footstepsModule = require(Modules:WaitForChild("FootstepsModule"))

-- // Functions
local function checkSpeed(humanoid)
	
	local walkSpeed = humanoid.WalkSpeed
	local moveDirection = humanoid.MoveDirection.Magnitude
	local floorMaterial = humanoid.FloorMaterial
	
	if walkSpeed > 0 and moveDirection > 0 and floorMaterial ~= Enum.Material.Air then
		return true
	end
	
	return false
end

local function getMaterial(material)
	local soundTable = footstepsModule:GetTableFromMaterial(material)
	
	if soundTable then
		local randomSound = footstepsModule:GetRandomSound(soundTable)
		
		if randomSound then
			return randomSound
		end
	end
	
	return nil
end

local function shootRay(rayOrigin, rayDirection, raycastParams)
	
	local raycastResult = workspace:Raycast(rayOrigin, rayDirection, raycastParams)
	
	if raycastResult then
		return raycastResult.Material
	end
	
	return nil
end

local function createFootstep(sound, character, rootPart)
	
	local rayOrigin = rootPart.Position
	local rayDirection = Vector3.new(0, -5, 0)
	
	local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new()
	raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
	raycastParams.IgnoreWater = false
	raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {character}
	
	local raycastResult = shootRay(rayOrigin, rayDirection, raycastParams)
	
	if raycastResult ~= nil then
		local newSound = getMaterial(raycastResult)
		sound.SoundId = newSound
		
		local newFootstep = sound:Clone()
		newFootstep.Name = "Footstep"
		newFootstep.PlaybackSpeed = math.random(9, 11) / 10
		
		newFootstep.Parent = rootPart
		
		newFootstep:Play()
		newFootstep.Ended:Connect(function()
			newFootstep:Destroy()
		end)
	end
	
end

-- // Events
playersService.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
	player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
		
		local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
		local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		
		-- Sound creation
		local footstepsSound = Instance.new("Sound")
		footstepsSound.Name = "FootstepTemplate"
		footstepsSound.Volume = 0.5
		
		footstepsSound.RollOffMode = Enum.RollOffMode.InverseTapered
		footstepsSound.RollOffMaxDistance = 35
		footstepsSound.RollOffMinDistance = 15
		
		footstepsSound.Parent = rootPart
		
		local cooldown = 0.4
		
		-- Main loop
		while humanoid.Health > 0 do
			task.wait(cooldown)
			
			if checkSpeed(humanoid) then
				createFootstep(footstepsSound, character, rootPart)
			end
		end
		
	end)
end)  -  Edit

-- Function to create blood effect
local function createBloodEffect(character)
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid then return end

    local function spewBlood()
        for i = 1, 10 do  -- Set amount of blood parts to release
            local bloodPart = Instance.new("Part")
            bloodPart.Size = Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1)
            bloodPart.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Bright red")
            bloodPart.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
            bloodPart.Anchored = false
            bloodPart.CanCollide = true
            bloodPart.CFrame = character:GetPivot() + Vector3.new(math.random(-5, 5), math.random(5, 5), math.random(-5, 5))
            bloodPart.Parent = Workspace
            -- Remove blood part after set time
			task.delay(5, function()
                bloodPart:Destroy()
            end)
        end
    end

    humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
        spewBlood()
    end)
end

-- Function to create blood effect
local function createBloodEffect(character)
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
    if not humanoid then return end

    local function spewBlood()
        for i = 1, 4 do
            local bloodPart = Instance.new("Part")
            bloodPart.Size = Vector3.new(1, 0.5, 1)
            bloodPart.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Bright red")
            bloodPart.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
            bloodPart.Anchored = false
            bloodPart.CanCollide = true
            bloodPart.CFrame = character:GetPivot() + Vector3.new(math.random(-1, 1), math.random(0, 0), math.random(-1, 1))
            bloodPart.Parent = Workspace
            -- Remove blood part after set time
            task.delay(5, function()
                bloodPart:Destroy()
            end)
        end
    end

    local lastHealth = humanoid.Health

    humanoid.HealthChanged:Connect(function(health)
        if health < lastHealth and health >= 15 then
            spewBlood()
        end
        lastHealth = health
    end)
end

    player.CharacterAdded:Connect(createBloodEffect)

local Players = game:GetService("Players")

--// Settings
local DECAL_ID = "rbxassetid://8228459691"
local bodyParts = {
	"Head",
	"Torso",
	"Left Arm",
	"Right Arm",
	"Left Leg",
	"Right Leg"

Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
	player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
		local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

		humanoid.BreakJointsOnDeath = false

		humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
			--// Ragdoll
			for _, joint in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
				if joint:IsA("Motor6D") then
					local socket = Instance.new("BallSocketConstraint")
					local a1 = Instance.new("Attachment")
					local a2 = Instance.new("Attachment")

					a1.Parent = joint.Part0
					a2.Parent = joint.Part1
					socket.Parent = joint.Parent
					socket.Attachment0 = a1
					socket.Attachment1 = a2
					a1.CFrame = joint.C0
					a2.CFrame = joint.C1
					socket.LimitsEnabled = true
					socket.TwistLimitsEnabled = true

					joint:Destroy()
				end
			end

			--// Add Decals to body parts
			for _, name in ipairs(bodyParts) do
				local part = character:FindFirstChild(name)
				if part and part:IsA("BasePart") then
					for _, face in ipairs(Enum.NormalId:GetEnumItems()) do
						local decal = Instance.new("Decal")
						decal.Texture = DECAL_ID
						decal.Face = face
						decal.Parent = part
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end)

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local Player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local IsShop = Remotes:WaitForChild("isShop")
local ShopEvent = Remotes:WaitForChild("ShopEvent")
local EquipEvent = Remotes:WaitForChild("EquipEvent")
-- NEW: use SettingsLoader instead of ShopModule
local ShopItems = require(ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Modules"):WaitForChild("SettingsLoader"))
local shiftLockModule = require(ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Modules"):WaitForChild("SmoothShiftLock"))


-- UI refs
local gui = Player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui"):WaitForChild("ScreenGui")

-- helpers
local function ForceDisableShiftLock()
	if shiftLockModule and shiftLockModule:IsEnabled() then
		shiftLockModule:ToggleShiftLock(false)
	end
	MainFrame.ShiftButton.Visible = false
	MainFrame.SprintButton.Visible = false
end


local function fadeCamera(fadeTime, zoomFOV, waitTime)
	if Player:FindFirstChild("inShop") and Player.inShop.Value == true then
		return
	end
	print("ASdfcvbdsdfa")
	fadeTime = fadeTime or 2
	zoomFOV = zoomFOV or 50
	local originalFOV = 70

	local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(fadeTime, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut)

	Frame.Visible = true


	local fadeIn = TweenService:Create(Frame, tweenInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 0})
	fadeIn:Play()

	local zoomIn = TweenService:Create(Camera, tweenInfo, {FieldOfView = zoomFOV})
	zoomIn:Play()

	fadeIn.Completed:Wait()

	task.wait(waitTime) 
	-- Fade out
	local fadeOut = TweenService:Create(Frame, tweenInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 1})
	fadeOut:Play()

	-- Zoom out
	local zoomOut = TweenService:Create(Camera, tweenInfo, {FieldOfView = originalFOV})
	zoomOut:Play()

	fadeOut.Completed:Wait()
	Frame.Visible = false
end

local function GetPlayerData()
	return Player:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
end

local function GetEquipped(category)
	local playerData = GetPlayerData()
	if not playerData then return "" end

	if category == "Killers" then
		local v = playerData:FindFirstChild("EquippedKiller")
		return v and v.Value or ""
	else
		local v = playerData:FindFirstChild("EquippedSurvivor")
		return v and v.Value or ""
	end
end

local function GetEquippedSkinForParent(parent)
	local playerData = GetPlayerData()
	if not playerData then return "" end

	if playerData:FindFirstChild("Killers") and playerData.Killers:FindFirstChild(parent) then
		local char = playerData.Killers:FindFirstChild(parent)
		local eq = char:FindFirstChild("EquippedSkin")
		return eq and eq.Value or ""
	end

	if playerData:FindFirstChild("Survivors") and playerData.Survivors:FindFirstChild(parent) then
		local char = playerData.Survivors:FindFirstChild(parent)
		local eq = char:FindFirstChild("EquippedSkin")
		return eq and eq.Value or ""
	end

	return ""
end

local function PlayerOwnsItem(category, itemName, parent)
	local playerData = GetPlayerData()
	if not playerData then return false end

	if category == "Skins" then
		if not parent then return false end
		local killers = playerData:FindFirstChild("Killers")
		if killers and killers:FindFirstChild(parent) then
			local skins = killers[parent]:FindFirstChild("Skins")
			return skins and skins:FindFirstChild(itemName) ~= nil
		end
		local surv = playerData:FindFirstChild("Survivors")
		if surv and surv:FindFirstChild(parent) then
			local skins = surv[parent]:FindFirstChild("Skins")
			return skins and skins:FindFirstChild(itemName) ~= nil
		end
		return false
	else
		local categoryFolder = playerData:FindFirstChild(category)
		if not categoryFolder then return false end
		return categoryFolder:FindFirstChild(itemName) ~= nil
	end
end

local function ClearItems()
	for _, item in pairs(ScrollingFrame:GetChildren()) do
		if item:IsA("ImageButton") and item.Name ~= "Template" then
			item:Destroy()
		end
	end
end

local function UpdatePurchaseButton(itemName, category, parent)
	if not itemName then
		PurchaseButton.Text = ""
		return
	end

	local cost
	if category == "Skins" then
		local skinsList = (ShopItems.Skins and ShopItems.Skins[parent]) or {}
		for _, s in ipairs(skinsList) do
			if s.Name == itemName then
				cost = s.Cost or 0
				break
			end
		end
	else
		for _, d in ipairs(ShopItems[category] or {}) do
			if d.Name == itemName then
				cost = d.Cost or 0
				break
			end
		end
	end

	local equipped, owned
	if category == "Skins" then
		equipped = GetEquippedSkinForParent(parent)
		owned = PlayerOwnsItem("Skins", itemName, parent)
	else
		equipped = GetEquipped(category)
		owned = PlayerOwnsItem(category, itemName)
	end

	if equipped == itemName then
		PurchaseButton.Text = "Equipped"
	elseif owned then
		PurchaseButton.Text = "Equip"
	else
		PurchaseButton.Text = tostring(cost or 0) .. "T"
	end
end

local function findCharacterModel(characterName, skinName)
	local charFolder = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Characters")

	local function searchFolder(folder)
		if not folder then return nil end
		local char = folder:FindFirstChild(characterName)
		if not char then return nil end

		if skinName and char:FindFirstChild(skinName) then
			return char:FindFirstChild(skinName)
		end

		if not skinName and char:FindFirstChild("Default") then
			return char:FindFirstChild("Default")
		end

		for _, child in ipairs(char:GetChildren()) do
			if child:IsA("Model") then
				return child
			end
		end
	end

	return
		searchFolder(charFolder)
		or searchFolder(charFolder:FindFirstChild("Killers"))
		or searchFolder(charFolder:FindFirstChild("Survivors"))
end

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
local playerChar = Player.Character or Player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = playerChar:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
local hrp = playerChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

Player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
	playerChar = char
	humanoid = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
	hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end)

local shopCam = workspace:WaitForChild("Shop"):WaitForChild("Camera")
local charSpawn = workspace:WaitForChild("Shop"):WaitForChild("CharacterSpawn")

local previewModel
local rotating = false

local function showPreviewCharacter(characterName, skinName)
	if previewModel then
		previewModel:Destroy()
		previewModel = nil
	end

	local template = findCharacterModel(characterName, skinName or "Default")
	if not template then
		NameLabel.Text = "Preview not found"
		return
	end

	previewModel = template:Clone()
	previewModel.Parent = workspace.Shop

	local hrp = previewModel:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if hrp then
		hrp.Anchored = true
	end

	if charSpawn then
		previewModel:PivotTo(charSpawn.CFrame)
	else
		previewModel:PivotTo(camera.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -5))
	end

	task.spawn(function()
		local humanoid = previewModel:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		if not humanoid then return end

		local idleValue = previewModel:FindFirstChild("IdleAnim")
		if not idleValue or not idleValue:IsA("StringValue") then return end

		local anim = Instance.new("Animation")
		anim.AnimationId = idleValue.Value

		local track = humanoid:LoadAnimation(anim)
		track.Looped = true
		track:Play()
	end)
end

-- Populate characters
local function PopulateItems(category)
	currentView = "Items"
	currentCategory = category
	currentSkinsParent = nil
	ClearItems()
	for _, data in ipairs(ShopItems[category] or {}) do
		local clone = Template:Clone()
		clone.Image = data.Image or ""
		clone.Visible = true
		clone.Parent = ScrollingFrame
		clone.Name = data.Name
		clone.TextLabel.Text = data.Name

		UpdatePurchaseButton(data.Name, category, nil)

		clone.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			selectedItem = data
			NameLabel.Text = data.Name
			DescriptionLabel.Text = data.Description
			UpdatePurchaseButton(data.Name, category, nil)
			showPreviewCharacter(data.Name, "Default")
		end)
	end
end

-- Populate skins for character
local function PopulateSkinsForCharacter(characterName)
	currentView = "Skins"
	currentSkinsParent = characterName
	ClearItems()

	local skinsList = (ShopItems.Skins and ShopItems.Skins[characterName]) or {}
	if #skinsList == 0 then
		NameLabel.Text = "No skins for " .. characterName
		selectedItem = nil
		showPreviewCharacter(characterName, "Default")
		return
	end

	for _, data in ipairs(skinsList) do
		local clone = Template:Clone()
		clone.Image = data.Image or data.SubImage or ""
		clone.Visible = true
		clone.Parent = ScrollingFrame
		clone.Name = data.Name
		clone.TextLabel.Text = data.Name

		UpdatePurchaseButton(data.Name, "Skins", characterName)

		clone.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			selectedItem = { Name = data.Name, Cost = data.Cost or 0, Parent = characterName }
			NameLabel.Text = data.Name
			DescriptionLabel.Text = data.Description
			UpdatePurchaseButton(data.Name, "Skins", characterName)
			showPreviewCharacter(characterName, data.Name)
		end)
	end

	local equipped = GetEquippedSkinForParent(characterName)
	NameLabel.Text = equipped ~= "" and equipped or "Default"
	selectedItem = nil

	showPreviewCharacter(characterName, equipped ~= "" and equipped or "Default")
end

local function UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped(category)
	if currentView == "Skins" and currentSkinsParent then
		local equippedSkin = GetEquippedSkinForParent(currentSkinsParent)
		NameLabel.Text = equippedSkin ~= "" and equippedSkin or "Default"
		selectedItem = nil
		showPreviewCharacter(currentSkinsParent, equippedSkin ~= "" and equippedSkin or "Default")
		return
	end

	local equippedName = GetEquipped(category)
	if equippedName == "" then
		NameLabel.Text = "No character equipped"
		PurchaseButton.Text = ""
		selectedItem = nil
		if previewModel then
			previewModel:Destroy()
			previewModel = nil
		end
		return
	end

	for _, data in ipairs(ShopItems[category] or {}) do
		if data.Name == equippedName then
			selectedItem = data
			NameLabel.Text = data.Name
			DescriptionLabel.Text = data.Description
			UpdatePurchaseButton(data.Name, category, nil)
			showPreviewCharacter(data.Name, "Default")
			break
		end
	end
end

local function UpdateTabHighlight()
	if currentCategory == "Killers" then
		KillersButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)
		SurvivorsButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(63,63,63)
	else
		KillersButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(63,63,63)
		SurvivorsButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)
	end
end

-- Events
PurchaseButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()

	if selectedItem then
		if currentView == "Skins" and currentSkinsParent then
			ShopEvent:FireServer(selectedItem, "Skins")
		else
			ShopEvent:FireServer(selectedItem, currentCategory)
		end
	end
end)

KillersButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	if not KillersButton.Active then return end
	currentView = "Items"
	currentCategory = "Killers"
	PopulateItems("Killers")
	UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped("Killers")
	UpdateTabHighlight()
end)

SurvivorsButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	if not SurvivorsButton.Active then return end
	currentView = "Items"
	currentCategory = "Survivors"
	PopulateItems("Survivors")
	UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped("Survivors")
	UpdateTabHighlight()
end)

if SkinsButton then
	SkinsButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		local parentChar

		if currentView == "Items" and selectedItem then
			parentChar = selectedItem.Name
		else
			parentChar = GetEquipped(currentCategory)
		end

		if not parentChar or parentChar == "" or not PlayerOwnsItem(currentCategory, parentChar) then
			return
		end

		PopulateSkinsForCharacter(parentChar)
		local equippedSkin = GetEquippedSkinForParent(parentChar)
		NameLabel.Text = equippedSkin
		DescriptionLabel.Text = ""
		PurchaseButton.Text = "Equipped"
		SkinsButton.Visible = false
		BackButton.Visible = true

		KillersButton.Active = false
		SurvivorsButton.Active = false
		KillersButton.AutoButtonColor = false
		SurvivorsButton.AutoButtonColor = false

		UpdateTabHighlight()
	end)
end

if BackButton then
	BackButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		SkinsButton.Visible = true
		BackButton.Visible = false
		KillersButton.Active = true
		SurvivorsButton.Active = true
		KillersButton.AutoButtonColor = true
		SurvivorsButton.AutoButtonColor = true
		PopulateItems(currentCategory)
		UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped(currentCategory)
		UpdateTabHighlight()
	end)
end

EquipEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(itemName, category, parent)
	if itemName == "NotEnoughTix" then
		PurchaseButton.Text = "Not enough Tix!"
		task.wait(1.4)
		if selectedItem then
			if currentView == "Skins" and parent then
				UpdatePurchaseButton(selectedItem.Name, "Skins", parent)
			else
				UpdatePurchaseButton(selectedItem.Name, currentCategory, nil)
			end
		end
		return
	end

	if category == "Skins" then
		if currentView == "Skins" and parent == currentSkinsParent then
			UpdatePurchaseButton(itemName, "Skins", parent)
			UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped(currentCategory)
		end
	else
		if selectedItem and selectedItem.Name == itemName then
			UpdatePurchaseButton(itemName, category, nil)
		end
		UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped(category)
	end
end)

ShopButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	ForceDisableShiftLock()
	IsShop:FireServer(true)

	task.spawn(function() fadeCamera(0.5, 50, 0.5) end)
	wait(0.4)
	ShopFrame.Visible = not ShopFrame.Visible
	ButtonsFrame.Visible = not ShopFrame.Visible

	if ShopFrame.Visible then
		PopulateItems(currentCategory)
		UpdateInfoFrameToEquipped(currentCategory)
		UpdateTabHighlight()

		camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable

		-- Replace static camera CFrame with dynamic mouse-tilt version
		local camPart = workspace.Shop:WaitForChild("Camera")
		local mouse = Player:GetMouse()
		local maxTilt = 10

		if _G.ShopCamConnection then
			_G.ShopCamConnection:Disconnect()

			camera.CFrame = camPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(
				math.rad((((mouse.Y - mouse.ViewSizeY / 2) / mouse.ViewSizeY) * -maxTilt)),
				math.rad((((mouse.X - mouse.ViewSizeX / 2) / mouse.ViewSizeX) * -maxTilt)),
				0
			)
		end)


		local equipped = GetEquipped(currentCategory)
		if equipped and equipped ~= "" then
			showPreviewCharacter(equipped, "Default")
		end
	else
		camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
		if humanoid then
			camera.CameraSubject = humanoid
		end
		if previewModel then
			previewModel:Destroy()
			previewModel = nil
		end
	end
end)

local function fadeCamera(fadeTime, zoomFOV, waitTime)
	if Player:FindFirstChild("InShop") and Player.InShop.Value == true then
		return
	end
	print("ASdfcvbdsdfa")
	fadeTime = fadeTime or 2
	zoomFOV = zoomFOV or 50
	local originalFOV = 70

	local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(fadeTime, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut)

	Frame.Visible = true


	local fadeIn = TweenService:Create(Frame, tweenInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 0})
	fadeIn:Play()

	local zoomIn = TweenService:Create(Camera, tweenInfo, {FieldOfView = zoomFOV})
	zoomIn:Play()
	
	fadeIn.Completed:Wait()
	
	task.wait(waitTime) 
	-- Fade out
	local fadeOut = TweenService:Create(Frame, tweenInfo, {BackgroundTransparency = 1})
	fadeOut:Play()

	-- Zoom out
	local zoomOut = TweenService:Create(Camera, tweenInfo, {FieldOfView = originalFOV})
	zoomOut:Play()

	fadeOut.Completed:Wait()
	Frame.Visible = false
end

-- Connect RemoteEvent
FadeCameraEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(fadeCamera)

  21:59:23.116  local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local Modules = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Modules")

local AbilityEvent = Remotes:WaitForChild("AbilityEvent")
local CharacterChanged = Remotes:WaitForChild("CharacterChanged")
local AbilityUnlock = Remotes:WaitForChild("AbilityUnlock")
local CharacterModule = require(Modules:WaitForChild("CharacterModule"))

local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local PlayerGui = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
local ScreenGui = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("ScreenGui")
local MainFrame = ScreenGui:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
local AbilitiesFrame = MainFrame:WaitForChild("AbilityFrame")

local abilityNames = {}
local abilityTemplates = {}
local cooldowns = {}
local currentClassType, currentCharacter = nil, nil

local inputLockedValue = player:WaitForChild("InputLocked")

-- Keyboard bindings (unchanged)
local killerKeybinds = {
	[Enum.KeyCode.Q] = 2,
	[Enum.KeyCode.E] = 3,
	[Enum.KeyCode.R] = 4,
}
local survivorKeybinds = {
	[Enum.KeyCode.Q] = 1,
	[Enum.KeyCode.E] = 2,
}

-- Gamepad bindings (console support)
local killerGamepadBinds = {
	[Enum.KeyCode.ButtonR2] = 1,          -- RT → ability 1 (was LMB)
	[Enum.KeyCode.ButtonX]  = 2,          -- X  → ability 2 (Q)
	[Enum.KeyCode.ButtonB]  = 3,          -- B  → ability 3 (E)
	[Enum.KeyCode.ButtonY]  = 4,          -- Y  → ability 4 (R)
}
local survivorGamepadBinds = {
	[Enum.KeyCode.ButtonX]  = 1,          -- X → ability 1 (Q)
	[Enum.KeyCode.ButtonB]  = 2,          -- B → ability 2 (E)
}

local function ClearAbilities()
	abilityNames = {}
	cooldowns = {}
	for _, btn in pairs(abilityTemplates) do
		btn:Destroy()
	end
	abilityTemplates = {}
end

local function UseAbility(index)
	if inputLockedValue.Value then
		return
	end

	if not abilityNames[index] then return end
	local abilityName = abilityNames[index]

	if cooldowns[index] ~= nil and tick() < cooldowns[index] then
		return
	end

	AbilityEvent:FireServer(currentClassType, currentCharacter, abilityName)

	local abilityModule = CharacterModule.GetAbilityModule(currentClassType, currentCharacter)
	local abilityData = abilityModule[abilityName]
	if abilityData then
		if abilityData.Cooldown then
			local cd = abilityData.Cooldown
			local abilityTemplate = abilityTemplates[index]
			local abilityIcon = abilityTemplate.AbilityIcon
			local cooldownLabel = abilityIcon.AbilityTimer

			cooldowns[index] = tick() + cd
			task.spawn(function()
				while cooldowns[index] ~= nil and tick() < cooldowns[index] do
					local remaining = cooldowns[index] - tick()
					cooldownLabel.Visible = true
					cooldownLabel.Text = string.format("%.1f", math.max(remaining, 0))
					abilityIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(102, 102, 102)
					task.wait(0.05)
				end
				cooldownLabel.Visible = false
				abilityIcon.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
			end)
		end
	end
end

local function BuildAbilityGui(classType, charName)
	ClearAbilities()
	currentClassType, currentCharacter = classType, charName
	if not classType or not charName then return end

	local abilityList = CharacterModule.GetAbilities(classType, charName)
	if not abilityList then return end
	local abilityModule = CharacterModule.GetAbilityModule(classType, charName)

	for i, abilityEntry in ipairs(abilityList) do
		local abilityName = abilityEntry.Name
		table.insert(abilityNames, abilityName)
		local abilityData = abilityModule[abilityName]
		if not abilityData then continue end

		local abilityTemplate = script.AbilityTemplate:Clone()
		abilityTemplate.Name = "Ability" .. i

		if classType == "Killer" and i == 1 then
			-- Show "M1" on PC but "RT" on console? We'll keep textual as generic
			abilityTemplate.AbilityKey.Text = "M1"  -- will be overridden for console in UI later? For now constant.
		else
			if classType == "Killer" then
				local keyMap = { [2] = "Q", [3] = "E", [4] = "R" }
				abilityTemplate.AbilityKey.Text = keyMap[i] or ""
			else
				local keyMap = { [1] = "Q", [2] = "E" }
				abilityTemplate.AbilityKey.Text = keyMap[i] or ""
			end
		end

		abilityTemplate.AbilityName.Text = abilityName
		abilityTemplate.AbilityIcon.Image = abilityData.ImageID
		abilityTemplate.AbilityIcon.AbilityTimer.Text = ""
		abilityTemplate.AbilityIcon.AbilityTimer.Visible = false
		abilityTemplate.Parent = AbilitiesFrame

		local index = i
		abilityTemplate.AbilityIcon.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if not inputLockedValue.Value then
				UseAbility(index)
			end
		end)

		abilityTemplates[i] = abilityTemplate
	end
end

local lastInputTime = 0
local inputCooldown = 0.15 

UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
	if gameProcessed then return end
	if inputLockedValue.Value then return end

	if tick() - lastInputTime < inputCooldown then
		return
	end
	lastInputTime = tick()

	-- Check gamepad first (specific buttons), then keyboard/mouse
	local gpIndex
	if currentClassType == "Killer" then
		gpIndex = killerGamepadBinds[input.KeyCode]
	elseif currentClassType == "Survivor" then
		gpIndex = survivorGamepadBinds[input.KeyCode]
	end

	if gpIndex then
		UseAbility(gpIndex)
		return
	end

	-- Legacy keyboard / mouse
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
		if currentClassType == "Killer" then
			UseAbility(1)
		end
		return
	end

	if currentClassType == "Killer" then
		local index = killerKeybinds[input.KeyCode]
		if index then
			UseAbility(index)
		end
	elseif currentClassType == "Survivor" then
		local index = survivorKeybinds[input.KeyCode]
		if index then
			UseAbility(index)
		end
	end
end)

CharacterChanged.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(classType, charName)
	BuildAbilityGui(classType, charName)
end)  -  Edit

local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local StatusEvent = Remotes:WaitForChild("StatusEvent")

local PlayerGui = Player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
local ScreenGui = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("ScreenGui")
local MainFrame = ScreenGui:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
local StatusFrame = MainFrame:WaitForChild("StatusFrame")

local effectLabels = {}
local connections = {}

local hiddenEffects = {
	["EndLag"] = true,
}

-- Roman numeral lookup (only up to 5)
local function toRoman(num)
	local lookup = {
		[1] = "I",
		[2] = "II",
		[3] = "III",
		[4] = "IV",
		[5] = "V",
	}
	return lookup[num] or tostring(num)
end

-- Clear all statuses (UI + countdowns)
local function clearAllStatuses()
	for effectName, frame in pairs(effectLabels) do
		if connections[effectName] then
			connections[effectName]:Disconnect()
			connections[effectName] = nil
		end
		frame:Destroy()
	end
	effectLabels = {}
end

if Player.Character then
	clearAllStatuses()
	local humanoid = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	if humanoid then
		humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
			clearAllStatuses()
		end)
	end
end

Player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(char)
	clearAllStatuses()
	local humanoid = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
	humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
		clearAllStatuses()
	end)
end)

-- Listen for server status updates
StatusEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(effectName, stacks, duration)
	if hiddenEffects[effectName] then return end

	if stacks > 0 then
		local frame = effectLabels[effectName]
		if not frame then
			frame = script.StatusTemplate:Clone()
			frame.Parent = StatusFrame
			effectLabels[effectName] = frame
		end

		local textLabel = frame.TextLabel
		local expireTime = tick() + duration

		-- Disconnect old countdown
		if connections[effectName] then
			connections[effectName]:Disconnect()
		end

		-- Start countdown
		connections[effectName] = game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			local remaining = math.max(0, math.ceil(expireTime - tick()))
			local roman = toRoman(stacks)
			textLabel.Text = effectName .. " " .. roman .. " (" .. remaining .. "s)"

			if remaining <= 0 then
				connections[effectName]:Disconnect()
				connections[effectName] = nil
				if effectLabels[effectName] then
					effectLabels[effectName]:Destroy()
					effectLabels[effectName] = nil
				end
			end
		end)

	else
		-- Remove a single status
		if effectLabels[effectName] then
			if connections[effectName] then
				connections[effectName]:Disconnect()
				connections[effectName] = nil
			end
			effectLabels[effectName]:Destroy()
			effectLabels[effectName] = nil
		end
	end
end)

  21:59:23.117  --// Services
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

--// Player
local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera

--// UI
local PlayerGui = Player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
local ScreenGui = PlayerGui:WaitForChild("ScreenGui")
local MainFrame = ScreenGui:WaitForChild("MainFrame")
local Frame = MainFrame:WaitForChild("BarFrame")
local HealthBar = Frame:WaitForChild("HealthBar")
local StaminaBar = Frame:WaitForChild("StaminaBar")
local SprintButton = MainFrame:WaitForChild("SprintButton")

--// Modules
local Modules = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Modules")
local Characters = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Characters")
local Killers = Characters:WaitForChild("Killers")
local Survivors = Characters:WaitForChild("Survivors")
local StatusManager = require(Modules:WaitForChild("StatusManager"))

--// Config
local NORMAL_FOV = 70
local SPRINT_FOV = 80
local FOV_TWEEN_TIME = 0.4
local MAX_STAT = 100
local STAMINA_DRAIN_RATE = 10
local STAMINA_REGEN_RATE = 20
local STAMINA_REGEN_DELAY = 0.3

--// State
local running = false
local sprintLocked = false
local shiftHeld = false
local mobileSprinting = false      -- for touch UI button
local gamepadSprint = false       -- toggled by left stick press
local stamina = MAX_STAT
local health = MAX_STAT
local lastSprintTime = 0

--// EndLag integration
local endlagMultiplierOverride = 1
local Remotes = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")
local SetEndLagMultiplier = Remotes:WaitForChild("SetEndLagMultiplier")

SetEndLagMultiplier.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(multiplier)
	endlagMultiplierOverride = multiplier
end)

--// Helpers
local function TweenFOV(target)
	TweenService:Create(Camera, TweenInfo.new(FOV_TWEEN_TIME, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {FieldOfView = target}):Play()
end

local function HasRole()
	return Player:FindFirstChild("Survivor") or Player:FindFirstChild("Killer")
end

local function IsAnchored()
	local char = Player.Character
	return char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and char.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored
end

local function GetBaseStats()
	local data = Player:WaitForChild("PlayerData")
	if Player:FindFirstChild("Killer") then
		return Killers:FindFirstChild(data.EquippedKiller.Value)
	elseif Player:FindFirstChild("Survivor") then
		return Survivors:FindFirstChild(data.EquippedSurvivor.Value)
	end
end

local function GetSprintSpeed()
	local base = GetBaseStats()
	if not base then return 16 end
	local haste = StatusManager.GetStacks("Haste") or 0
	return base.SprintSpeed.Value + (3 * haste)
end

local function GetWalkSpeed()
	local base = GetBaseStats()
	if not base then return 16 end
	return base.WalkSpeed.Value
end

--// Sprint Functions
local function StartSprint()
	if not HasRole() or sprintLocked or running then return end
	local humanoid = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	if not humanoid or humanoid.MoveDirection.Magnitude == 0 then return end
	if Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyVelocity") then return end
	running = true
	lastSprintTime = tick()
	TweenFOV(SPRINT_FOV)
end

local function StopSprint()
	if not running then return end
	running = false
	lastSprintTime = tick()
	TweenFOV(NORMAL_FOV)
end

--// Toggle sprint (used by gamepad stick press)
local function ToggleSprint()
	if running then
		StopSprint()
	else
		StartSprint()
	end
end

--// UI Updates
local function UpdateHealthBar()
	local humanoid = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	if humanoid then
		health = humanoid.Health
		MAX_STAT = humanoid.MaxHealth
	end
	local ratio = math.clamp(health / MAX_STAT, 0, 1)
	HealthBar.Frame.Size = UDim2.new(ratio, 0, 1, 0)
	HealthBar.HealthText.Text = string.format("%d/%d", math.floor(health), MAX_STAT)
	HealthBar.HealthText.TextColor3 = ratio <= 0.25 and Color3.new(1, 0, 0) or Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
end

local function UpdateStaminaBar()
	local ratio = math.clamp(stamina / 100, 0, 1)
	StaminaBar.Frame.Size = UDim2.new(ratio, 0, 1, 0)
	StaminaBar.StaminaText.Text = string.format("%d/%d", math.floor(stamina), 100)
	StaminaBar.StaminaText.TextColor3 = ratio <= 0.25 and Color3.new(1, 0, 0) or Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
end

--// Input
if UserInputService.TouchEnabled then
	SprintButton.Visible = true
else
	SprintButton.Visible = false
end

UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
	if processed then return end

	-- Keyboard
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then
		shiftHeld = true
		StartSprint()
		return
	end

	-- Gamepad: Left Stick press toggles sprint
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.ButtonL3 then
		ToggleSprint()
		return
	end
end)

UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
	if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then
		shiftHeld = false
		StopSprint()
	end
end)

SprintButton.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
	if not mobileSprinting then
		mobileSprinting = true
		StartSprint()
	else
		mobileSprinting = false
		StopSprint()
	end
end)


--// Core Loop
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
	local humanoid = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	if not humanoid then return end

	UpdateHealthBar()

	local walkSpeedIsZero = humanoid.WalkSpeed == 0

	local slownessStacks = StatusManager.GetStacks("Slowness") or 0
	local hasteStacks = StatusManager.GetStacks("Haste") or 0

	local reductionPerStack = 0.3
	local boostPerStack = 0.07

	local isMoving = humanoid.MoveDirection.Magnitude > 0
	local isSprinting = (running or mobileSprinting) and not IsAnchored() and not walkSpeedIsZero

	if isSprinting then
		local sprintSpeed = GetSprintSpeed()
		if slownessStacks > 0 then
			sprintSpeed = sprintSpeed * (1 - reductionPerStack * slownessStacks)
		elseif hasteStacks > 0 then
			sprintSpeed = sprintSpeed * (1 + boostPerStack * hasteStacks)
		end

		sprintSpeed = sprintSpeed * endlagMultiplierOverride
		humanoid.WalkSpeed = math.max(1, sprintSpeed)

		if isMoving then
			stamina = math.clamp(stamina - (STAMINA_DRAIN_RATE * dt), 0, 100)
			lastSprintTime = tick()
		else
			if tick() - lastSprintTime >= STAMINA_REGEN_DELAY then
				stamina = math.clamp(stamina + (STAMINA_REGEN_RATE * dt), 0, 100)
			end
		end

		UpdateStaminaBar()

		if stamina <= 0 then
			sprintLocked = true
			StopSprint()
			mobileSprinting = false
			gamepadSprint = false
		end
	else
		if stamina < 100 and (tick() - lastSprintTime >= STAMINA_REGEN_DELAY) then
			stamina = math.clamp(stamina + (STAMINA_REGEN_RATE * dt), 0, 100)
			UpdateStaminaBar()
			if stamina >= 10 then
				sprintLocked = false
			end
		end

		if not walkSpeedIsZero then
			local walkSpeed = GetWalkSpeed()
			if slownessStacks > 0 then
				walkSpeed = walkSpeed * (1 - reductionPerStack * slownessStacks)
			elseif hasteStacks > 0 then
				walkSpeed = walkSpeed * (1 + boostPerStack * hasteStacks)
			end

			walkSpeed = walkSpeed * endlagMultiplierOverride
			humanoid.WalkSpeed = math.max(1, walkSpeed)
		end
	end
end)  -  Edit

local function ForceDisableShiftLock()
	if shiftLockModule and shiftLockModule:IsEnabled() then
		shiftLockModule:ToggleShiftLock(false)
	end
	MainFrame.ShiftButton.Visible = false
	MainFrame.SprintButton.Visible = false

end

local function FadeInLabel(label, duration, textOnly)
	local info = TweenInfo.new(duration, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
	label.TextTransparency = 1

	if not textOnly then
		label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		TweenService:Create(label, info, {
			TextTransparency = 0,
			BackgroundTransparency = 0.65
		}):Play()
	else
		TweenService:Create(label, info, {
			TextTransparency = 0
		}):Play()
	end
end

local function FadeInIntroSequence()
	local roundText = IntroGui:WaitForChild("RoundText")
	local duration = 1.5

	FadeInLabel(roundText, duration, true)
	task.wait(duration + 0.2)

	for _, label in pairs(IntroGui:GetChildren()) do
		if label:IsA("TextLabel") and label ~= roundText then
			FadeInLabel(label, 1)
		end
	end
end


local function PlayCutscene(folder, equippedkiller, killer)
	ForceDisableShiftLock()
	if player:FindFirstChild("InShop") and player.InShop.Value == true then
		return
	end
	
	print(folder)
	script.Sound:Play()
	
	local cam = folder:WaitForChild("Camera")
	local char = folder:WaitForChild("Character")
	local animcam = folder:WaitForChild("CameraAnimation").Value
	local animchar = folder:WaitForChild("CharacterAnimation").Value

	print("Cutscene start")

	repeat task.wait() until player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	repeat task.wait() until workspace.CurrentCamera

	MainFrame.Visible = false

	local oldCameraType = camera.CameraType
	local oldCameraSubject = camera.CameraSubject

	camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable
	camera.CFrame = cam.FakeCam.CFrame

	local camController = cam:WaitForChild("AnimationController")
	local camAnimator = camController:WaitForChild("Animator")

	local camAnim = Instance.new("Animation")
	camAnim.AnimationId = animcam
	local camTrack = camAnimator:LoadAnimation(camAnim)
	camTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action

	local charAnim = Instance.new("Animation")
	charAnim.AnimationId = animchar
	local charTrack = char.Humanoid:LoadAnimation(charAnim)
	charTrack.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action

	IntroGui.RoundText.Visible = true
	IntroGui.KillerText.Text = equippedkiller
	IntroGui.PlayerText.Text = "@" .. killer
	IntroGui.Visible = true

	task.spawn(FadeInIntroSequence)

	camTrack:Play()
	charTrack:Play()

--	task.spawn(function()
--		charTrack:GetMarkerReachedSignal("Hit"):Wait()
--		folder.Sound:Play()
--	end)


	local heartbeatConn
	heartbeatConn = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
		camera.CFrame = cam.FakeCam.CFrame
	end)

	camTrack.Stopped:Wait()

	heartbeatConn:Disconnect()
	charTrack:Stop()

	if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
		camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
		camera.CameraSubject = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	else
		repeat task.wait() until player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
		camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Custom
		camera.CameraSubject = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	end

	IntroGui.Visible = false
	MainFrame.Visible = true

	for _, label in pairs(IntroGui:GetChildren()) do
		if label:IsA("TextLabel")  then
			label.TextTransparency = 1
			label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		end
	end	
	
	print("Cutscene end")
	if UserInputService.TouchEnabled then
		MainFrame.ShiftButton.Visible = true
		MainFrame.SprintButton.Visible = true
	end
end

IntroRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(PlayCutscene)  -  Edit

  21:59:23.123  local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

local function disableDoors()
	local map = workspace:FindFirstChild("Map")
	if not map then return end

	local folder = map:FindFirstChild("KillerOnlyDoors")
	if not folder then return end

	for _, part in ipairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
		if part:IsA("BasePart") then
			part.CanCollide = false
		end
	end

	if not folder:FindFirstChild("__Connected") then
		local tag = Instance.new("BoolValue")
		tag.Name = "__Connected"
		tag.Parent = folder

		folder.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
			if child:IsA("BasePart") then
				child.CanCollide = false
			end
		end)
	end
end

local function enableDoors()
	local map = workspace:FindFirstChild("Map")
	if not map then return end

	local folder = map:FindFirstChild("KillerOnlyDoors")
	if not folder then return end

	for _, part in ipairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
		if part:IsA("BasePart") then
			part.CanCollide = true
		end
	end
end

player.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
	if child.Name == "Killer" then
		disableDoors()
	end
end)

player.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
	if child.Name == "Killer" then
		enableDoors()
	end
end)

if player:FindFirstChild("Killer") then
	disableDoors()
end
